Pre-empted traps for implementers are\n9: added at decompose time.\n10: \n11: ## Pre-empted traps (read before executing ANY task)\n12: \n13: Carried forward from `vk-swarm-node-foundations` (same repo, same gate) + hive/Postgres analogues. The\n14: node-foundations ledger is the authority for the originals; condensed here.\n15: \n16: ### Trap 1 — WAI gate is TypeScript-shaped; this is a Cargo workspace\n17: Every Rust task sets BOTH in its `## Done when`: `WAI_TYPECHECK_CMD=\"cargo check -p <crate>\"` (or\n18: `--workspace` when arms span crates) and `WAI_TEST_CMD=\"cargo test -p <crate> <test_name>\"`. Omitting\n19: them runs the wrong/no check — a hollow pass.\n20: \n21: ### Trap 2 — SQLx OFFLINE on the node (SQLite) side; build against a live migrated DB\n22: Committed `.sqlx` cache + unset `DATABASE_URL` → `query!` validates against the cache, not a live DB.\n23: Tasks adding a migration + new query export `DATABASE_URL=sqlite://<repo>/dev_assets/db.sqlite` against\n24: a migrated dev DB. **Never run `cargo sqlx prepare` in a gated task** (it rewrites tracked `.sqlx/*.json`\n25: the gate's file-allow-list rejects). Regenerate once at `/wai:close`.\n26: \n27: ### Trap 2b — Hive (Postgres / `crates/remote`) query validation + tests need a LIVE Postgres (confirmed)\n28: Confirmed in code: the remote crate's `query!`/`query_as!` validate against the **shared root `.sqlx`\n29: offline cache** (same cache as the node side). Adding/changing a Postgres query therefore needs a live\n30: `DATABASE_URL`/`SERVER_DATABASE_URL` pointed at a **migrated Postgres** (`crates/remote/src/config.rs:45`)\n31: OR a cache regen — it will NOT validate against the SQLite dev DB. **And hive integration tests SKIP\n32: without a DB:** `crates/remote/tests/backfill_e2e.rs` uses `skip_without_db!` (returns early if\n33: `DATABASE_URL` unset); the hermetic SQLite `db::test_utils::create_test_pool()` does **not** apply to\n34: the hive. **Consequence for every hive-side task (102, 107, and all of P2/P3/P6/P7 hive work):** its\n35: `scope_test` is a `#[tokio::test]` that REQUIRES `DATABASE_URL=postgres://…` against a migrated PG, or\n36: the WAI gate runs a SKIPPED test and reports a **hollow pass**. The executor MUST stand up a Postgres\n37: (migrated via `sqlx::migrate!(\"./migrations\")`, `crates/remote/src/db/mod.rs:51`) and export\n38: `DATABASE_URL` before running any hive task. A hive task with no Postgres precondition + a skip-guarded\n39: test is NOT verifiable — flag such tasks. (This is genuinely harder than node-foundations, which never\n40: touched the remote crate. If a CI Postgres is not readily available, raise it before executing P-hive\n41: tasks.)\n42: \n43: ### Trap 3 — `enum_dispatch` / WS-message exhaustiveness on BOTH ends\n44: Adding a `NodeMessage` or `ServerMessage` variant (op-log op, durable ack, heartbeat, lease grant)\n45: forces editing **every** match arm on that end in the SAME commit or the workspace won't compile under\n46: `-D warnings`. The node side (`hive_client.rs`/`hive_sync.rs`/`node_runner.rs`) AND the hive side\n47: (`crates/remote` WS dispatch) each have their own exhaustive match sites — a new variant is a single\n48: cohesive `mixed` task per end (or one cross-cutting task), not a create+wire split. Anchor list of arms\n49: is filled from the hive-side anchor investigation.\n50: \n51: ### Trap 4 — Know which crate owns the logic (no cross-crate inversion)\n52: `services` does not depend on `local-deployment`; trait methods dispatch into the impl. Confirm the\n53: owning crate/trait for each touched function before authoring (the node-foundations recovery work lived\n54: in the `services` trait, not `local-deployment`). For hive logic, confirm `crates/remote` ownership.\n55: \n56: ### Trap 5 — Anchor-checker strips `crates/*/` (precheck false-positive) — already hit\n57: See Precheck notes below. Recorded so a precheck re-run is not mistaken for a real contradiction.\n58: \n59: ### Trap 6 — Frozen spec; escalate scope discoveries to the user\n60: The spec is frozen at precheck (ADR-0001). A spec-vs-reality contradiction or an entangled/oversized\n61: area discovered during decompose is **escalated to the user**, never papered over with a vague task or\n62: a silent spec edit — exactly how node-foundations carved out `vk-swarm-node-ui-localize`. The SC1\n63: central-UI carve (see plan Scope note) follows this protocol.\n64: \n65: ## Decompose decisions (2026-06-30)\n66: \n67: ### USER-APPROVED SCOPE SPLIT — SC1 central-management UI → `vk-swarm-hive-ui`\n68: Decompose found SC1 has two separable halves: (a) the **data-plane** guarantee \"no node↔node /\n69: node↔hive↔node fan-out\", and (b) the **hive web UI manages all** cross-node tasks/attempts/executions.\n70: Half (b) is a workstream-scale frontend build (the hive UI today is a 4-page auth stub; the\n71: management UI lives in the *node* frontend; cross-node task/attempt/execution views are net-new). **User\n72: decision (2026-06-30): carve half (b) into `vk-swarm-hive-ui`** (tracker seeded, no spec yet). This\n73: workstream covers SC2–SC7 + SC1's data-plane half (phase-6). SC1 stays in the frozen spec, claimed by\n74: phase-6; the UI deferral is recorded here — **no spec edit** (mirrors the node-foundations →\n75: `vk-swarm-node-ui-localize` carve).\n76: \n77: ### Finding — SC1 \"no fan-out of shared task state\" is LARGELY ALREADY SATISFIED\n78: Verified in code: the hive's node-facing broadcast (`ConnectionManager::send_to_nodes`/`broadcast_to_org`,\n79: `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/connection.rs:138,189`) carries **only** `ProjectSync` and `NodeRemoved` —\n80: it does **not** push shared-*task* state to nodes today. The shared-task fan-out that exists\n81: (`electric_proxy.rs` `GET /v1/shape/shared_tasks` + `ActivityBroker`, `crates/remote/src/activity/broker.rs:48`)\n82: targets **browsers** (which the hive UI needs). **Therefore phase-6 (SC1 data-plane) is \"verify + guard\n83: against regression + keep the node-facing channel assignment-only,\" not \"remove a large fan-out.\"** This\n84: is surfaced (not a contradiction): SC1's data-plane intent is met by construction; the task asserts and\n85: fences it. Browser-facing fan-out (electric_proxy/broker) is OUT of scope for \"no fan-out\" — it is the\n86: hive-UI data source.\n87: \n88: ### Decompose decision — WS protocol enums are hand-duplicated; DUAL-EDIT, do not deduplicate (this workstream)\n89: `NodeMessage`/`HiveMessage` are defined **twice** — hive `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/message.rs:15,91`\n90: and node `crates/services/src/services/hive_client.rs:82,123` — and have **already drifted** (`Deregister`\n91: exists hive-side only). Every new variant (op-log op, durable ack, heartbeat, lease grant) is added to\n92: **both** copies in the same commit (Trap 3). **Decision:** keep the dual-definition convention and add\n93: variants to both — deduplicating into a shared protocol crate is hygiene OUT of scope here (it would be\n94: a large cross-crate move touching every match site). Each protocol task is a single cohesive `mixed`\n95: task editing both crates + the exhaustive hive match (`session.rs:512`) + an explicit node arm **before\n96: the `_ =>` wildcard at `hive_client.rs:1062`** (the wildcard silently drops unhandled hive→node variants\n97: — the #1 easy-to-miss bug here).\n98: \n99: ### Decompose decision — durable-ack emission requires threading `ws_sender` into apply handlers\n100: Hive apply handlers `handle_attempt_sync`/`handle_execution_sync`/`handle_logs_batch`\n101: (`session.rs:1188,1307,1388`) currently take `node_id`/`pool` only — **not** the WS sender. Emitting a\n102: durable per-op ack (the SC2c fix) requires threading `ws_sender` into those signatures. `handle_task_sync`\n103: (session.rs:1547, replies `TaskSyncResponse`) and `handle_heartbeat` (replies `HeartbeatAck`,\n104: session.rs:607) are the existing templates. The op-log apply is a NEW `handle_op_batch` handler beside\n105: them; acks reuse the `HeartbeatAck` send shape.\n106: \n107: ### Decompose decision — PHASE-BY-PHASE authoring (user-approved)\n108: This decompose authors **Phase 1 (the op-log foundation) only**; later phases are authored in subsequent\n109: `/wai:decompose` passes as each prior ships (user decision 2026-06-30). Consequence for the gate:\n110: `wai-plan-lint` reads ALL spec SC ids from the token and will report SC1,SC3–SC7 **unclaimed** until\n111: their phases are authored — this is **expected-pending**, not a lint failure to paper over. Phase 1's\n112: internal consistency (plan↔frontmatter deps/conflicts, verification present, failing-tests-first) IS\n113: enforced now. A full PLAN-LINT PASS is achieved only when the final phase is authored.\n114: \n115: ## Phase-1 authoring — ratified judgment calls + tracer limitations (2026-06-30)\n116: \n117: The Phase-1 author surfaced six judgment calls (Trap 6). Ratified after review:\n118: \n119: 1. **106 parks on project-link-absent, not parent-task-absent** — RATIFIED. `upsert_from_node`\n120:    (`tasks.rs:566`) has no parent-task FK; the real transient dependency is the ProjectsSync link, which\n121:    `handle_task_sync` already encodes. Correct reading of SC2b at the task tier.\n122: 2. **106 splits PARK (transient, `node_local_projects` row absent) vs SKIP+ADVANCE (permanent,\n123:    not swarm-linked)** — RATIFIED, and load-bearing. Because 105 enqueues for ALL projects (the `db`\n124:    crate can't cheaply do the swarm lookup), a non-swarm task at the outbox head would park *permanently*\n125:    and wedge the cursor if \"not linked\" parked. The split (encoded as 106's third test) prevents the\n126:    wedge. This mirrors `handle_task_sync`'s three-branch resolution.\n127: 3. **105 idempotency_key = `task:{id}:{uuid}` (per-write-unique, persisted on the op row), NOT\n128:    `task:{id}:{version}`** — RATIFIED. `Task::update` (`queries.rs:305`) bumps no version, so a\n129:    version-key would self-collide and `UNIQUE(idempotency_key)` would silently drop updates. A re-sent\n130:    op reuses its stored key → hive dedups. (Same no-version fact as ADR-0007's dirty-guard motivation.)\n131: 4. **105 enqueue is best-effort, non-atomic** with the task write (callers hold `&SqlitePool`, not a\n132:    txn) — RATIFIED as a TRACER LIMITATION. The legacy sync path is the backstop. **Consequence:\n133:    Phase-1-tracer does NOT fully satisfy SC2c \"zero silent write loss\" — true no-loss needs the enqueue\n134:    in the SAME transaction as the entity write** (threading a txn through the ~8 `Task::create` callers),\n135:    which is the next Phase-1 increment. SC2c is *claimed* by 102/106/108 (the durable-ack mechanism) but\n136:    the no-loss guarantee is only fully closed by the transactional enqueue.\n137: 5. **108 advances the cursor via a new `HiveEvent::OpAck`** consumed in `run_node_runner` (which holds\n138:    the pool), mirroring the `TaskSyncResponse`/`BackfillRequest` \"DB write happens in run_node_runner\"\n139:    pattern — RATIFIED. `HiveEvent` has no third/cross-crate match site (grep-verified), so 108's `files:`\n140:    (hive_client.rs + node_runner.rs) is complete.\n141: 6. **Trap 2b (Postgres) applies to 102 + 106** — RATIFIED; each states the live-PG precondition.\n142: \n143: **Honest SC2 status after Phase-1-tracer:** the ordered, acknowledged round-trip *mechanism* is proven\n144: (SC2a single ordered channel — additive, alongside legacy; SC2b parent/link-before-child parking; SC2c\n145: durable per-op ack + cursor-advance-only-on-ack). NOT yet done: transactional enqueue (full SC2c\n146: no-loss), attempt/exec/log op types, and retirement of the five legacy push paths. These are tracked as\n147: the next Phase-1 increment in plan.md.\n148: \n149: ## Phase-1 sibling-advisory acknowledgement (wai-plan-lint `W:` lines, SC6)\n150: \n151: - **101 `…_add_node_outbox.sql` beside `…_init.sql`** — migrations are independent forward-only DDL, NOT\n152:   reimplementations of a pattern. Authored to house conventions confirmed against the recent\n153:   `queued_messages` migration (BLOB UUID PKs, `datetime('now','subsec')`, `CREATE … IF NOT EXISTS`,\n154:   partial index). Not a pattern sibling.\n155: - **102 `…_add_node_op_log.sql` beside `…_shared_tasks_activity.sql`** — same: independent Postgres DDL,\n156:   not a pattern sibling. **102's test `node_op_log_migration.rs` beside `backfill_e2e.rs` IS a real\n157:   sibling** — the task reads it and reuses its `database_url()`/`skip_without_db!`/`create_pool()`\n158:   helpers verbatim (no shared `common` module exists). Acknowledged, handled in-task.\n159: - **104 `node_outbox.rs` beside `activity_dismissal.rs`** — the task carries a `## Sibling alignment`\n160:   step reading an existing `db` model (`draft.rs`) for trait surface / error type / test style. The\n161:   genuine pattern sibling is read; `activity_dismissal.rs` is one of many same-dir models, not the\n162:   authority. Acknowledged.\n163: \n164: ## Phase-1 lint status (expected-pending, not a failure to paper over)\n165: After the Phase-1 fixes (SC2/TS1 claimed; clause sub-ids SC2a/b/c are colon-less PROSE in the spec so\n166: the lint's declared id is `SC2`), `wai-plan-lint` reports only **SC1, SC3–SC7 and TS2–TS7 unclaimed** —\n167: the unauthored phases. Pre-empted traps for implementers are\nadded at decompose time.\n\n## Pre-empted traps (read before executing ANY task)\n\nCarried forward from `vk-swarm-node-foundations` (same repo, same gate) + hive/Postgres analogues. The\nnode-foundations ledger is the authority for the originals; condensed here.\n\n### Trap 1 — WAI gate is TypeScript-shaped; this is a Cargo workspace\nEvery Rust task sets BOTH in its `## Done when`: `WAI_TYPECHECK_CMD=\"cargo check -p <crate>\"` (or\n`--workspace` when arms span crates) and `WAI_TEST_CMD=\"cargo test -p <crate> <test_name>\"`. Omitting\nthem runs the wrong/no check — a hollow pass.\n\n### Trap 2 — SQLx OFFLINE on the node (SQLite) side; build against a live migrated DB\nCommitted `.sqlx` cache + unset `DATABASE_URL` → `query!` validates against the cache, not a live DB.\nTasks adding a migration + new query export `DATABASE_URL=sqlite://<repo>/dev_assets/db.sqlite` against\na migrated dev DB. **Never run `cargo sqlx prepare` in a gated task** (it rewrites tracked `.sqlx/*.json`\nthe gate's file-allow-list rejects). Regenerate once at `/wai:close`.\n\n### Trap 2b — Hive (Postgres / `crates/remote`) query validation + tests need a LIVE Postgres (confirmed)\nConfirmed in code: the remote crate's `query!`/`query_as!` validate against the **shared root `.sqlx`\noffline cache** (same cache as the node side). Adding/changing a Postgres query therefore needs a live\n`DATABASE_URL`/`SERVER_DATABASE_URL` pointed at a **migrated Postgres** (`crates/remote/src/config.rs:45`)\nOR a cache regen — it will NOT validate against the SQLite dev DB. **And hive integration tests SKIP\nwithout a DB:** `crates/remote/tests/backfill_e2e.rs` uses `skip_without_db!` (returns early if\n`DATABASE_URL` unset); the hermetic SQLite `db::test_utils::create_test_pool()` does **not** apply to\nthe hive. **Consequence for every hive-side task (102, 107, and all of P2/P3/P6/P7 hive work):** its\n`scope_test` is a `#[tokio::test]` that REQUIRES `DATABASE_URL=postgres://…` against a migrated PG, or\nthe WAI gate runs a SKIPPED test and reports a **hollow pass**. The executor MUST stand up a Postgres\n(migrated via `sqlx::migrate!(\"./migrations\")`, `crates/remote/src/db/mod.rs:51`) and export\n`DATABASE_URL` before running any hive task. A hive task with no Postgres precondition + a skip-guarded\ntest is NOT verifiable — flag such tasks. (This is genuinely harder than node-foundations, which never\ntouched the remote crate. If a CI Postgres is not readily available, raise it before executing P-hive\ntasks.)\n\n### Trap 3 — `enum_dispatch` / WS-message exhaustiveness on BOTH ends\nAdding a `NodeMessage` or `ServerMessage` variant (op-log op, durable ack, heartbeat, lease grant)\nforces editing **every** match arm on that end in the SAME commit or the workspace won't compile under\n`-D warnings`. The node side (`hive_client.rs`/`hive_sync.rs`/`node_runner.rs`) AND the hive side\n(`crates/remote` WS dispatch) each have their own exhaustive match sites — a new variant is a single\ncohesive `mixed` task per end (or one cross-cutting task), not a create+wire split. Anchor list of arms\nis filled from the hive-side anchor investigation.\n\n### Trap 4 — Know which crate owns the logic (no cross-crate inversion)\n`services` does not depend on `local-deployment`; trait methods dispatch into the impl. Confirm the\nowning crate/trait for each touched function before authoring (the node-foundations recovery work lived\nin the `services` trait, not `local-deployment`). For hive logic, confirm `crates/remote` ownership.\n\n### Trap 5 — Anchor-checker strips `crates/*/` (precheck false-positive) — already hit\nSee Precheck notes below. Recorded so a precheck re-run is not mistaken for a real contradiction.\n\n### Trap 6 — Frozen spec; escalate scope discoveries to the user\nThe spec is frozen at precheck (ADR-0001). A spec-vs-reality contradiction or an entangled/oversized\narea discovered during decompose is **escalated to the user**, never papered over with a vague task or\na silent spec edit — exactly how node-foundations carved out `vk-swarm-node-ui-localize`. The SC1\ncentral-UI carve (see plan Scope note) follows this protocol.\n\n## Decompose decisions (2026-06-30)\n\n### USER-APPROVED SCOPE SPLIT — SC1 central-management UI → `vk-swarm-hive-ui`\nDecompose found SC1 has two separable halves: (a) the **data-plane** guarantee \"no node↔node /\nnode↔hive↔node fan-out\", and (b) the **hive web UI manages all** cross-node tasks/attempts/executions.\nHalf (b) is a workstream-scale frontend build (the hive UI today is a 4-page auth stub; the\nmanagement UI lives in the *node* frontend; cross-node task/attempt/execution views are net-new). **User\ndecision (2026-06-30): carve half (b) into `vk-swarm-hive-ui`** (tracker seeded, no spec yet). This\nworkstream covers SC2–SC7 + SC1's data-plane half (phase-6). SC1 stays in the frozen spec, claimed by\nphase-6; the UI deferral is recorded here — **no spec edit** (mirrors the node-foundations →\n`vk-swarm-node-ui-localize` carve).\n\n### Finding — SC1 \"no fan-out of shared task state\" is LARGELY ALREADY SATISFIED\nVerified in code: the hive's node-facing broadcast (`ConnectionManager::send_to_nodes`/`broadcast_to_org`,\n`crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/connection.rs:138,189`) carries **only** `ProjectSync` and `NodeRemoved` —\nit does **not** push shared-*task* state to nodes today. The shared-task fan-out that exists\n(`electric_proxy.rs` `GET /v1/shape/shared_tasks` + `ActivityBroker`, `crates/remote/src/activity/broker.rs:48`)\ntargets **browsers** (which the hive UI needs). **Therefore phase-6 (SC1 data-plane) is \"verify + guard\nagainst regression + keep the node-facing channel assignment-only,\" not \"remove a large fan-out.\"** This\nis surfaced (not a contradiction): SC1's data-plane intent is met by construction; the task asserts and\nfences it. Browser-facing fan-out (electric_proxy/broker) is OUT of scope for \"no fan-out\" — it is the\nhive-UI data source.\n\n### Decompose decision — WS protocol enums are hand-duplicated; DUAL-EDIT, do not deduplicate (this workstream)\n`NodeMessage`/`HiveMessage` are defined **twice** — hive `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/message.rs:15,91`\nand node `crates/services/src/services/hive_client.rs:82,123` — and have **already drifted** (`Deregister`\nexists hive-side only). Every new variant (op-log op, durable ack, heartbeat, lease grant) is added to\n**both** copies in the same commit (Trap 3). **Decision:** keep the dual-definition convention and add\nvariants to both — deduplicating into a shared protocol crate is hygiene OUT of scope here (it would be\na large cross-crate move touching every match site). Each protocol task is a single cohesive `mixed`\ntask editing both crates + the exhaustive hive match (`session.rs:512`) + an explicit node arm **before\nthe `_ =>` wildcard at `hive_client.rs:1062`** (the wildcard silently drops unhandled hive→node variants\n— the #1 easy-to-miss bug here).\n\n### Decompose decision — durable-ack emission requires threading `ws_sender` into apply handlers\nHive apply handlers `handle_attempt_sync`/`handle_execution_sync`/`handle_logs_batch`\n(`session.rs:1188,1307,1388`) currently take `node_id`/`pool` only — **not** the WS sender. Emitting a\ndurable per-op ack (the SC2c fix) requires threading `ws_sender` into those signatures. `handle_task_sync`\n(session.rs:1547, replies `TaskSyncResponse`) and `handle_heartbeat` (replies `HeartbeatAck`,\nsession.rs:607) are the existing templates. The op-log apply is a NEW `handle_op_batch` handler beside\nthem; acks reuse the `HeartbeatAck` send shape.\n\n### Decompose decision — PHASE-BY-PHASE authoring (user-approved)\nThis decompose authors **Phase 1 (the op-log foundation) only**; later phases are authored in subsequent\n`/wai:decompose` passes as each prior ships (user decision 2026-06-30). Consequence for the gate:\n`wai-plan-lint` reads ALL spec SC ids from the token and will report SC1,SC3–SC7 **unclaimed** until\ntheir phases are authored — this is **expected-pending**, not a lint failure to paper over. Phase 1's\ninternal consistency (plan↔frontmatter deps/conflicts, verification present, failing-tests-first) IS\nenforced now. A full PLAN-LINT PASS is achieved only when the final phase is authored.\n\n## Phase-1 authoring — ratified judgment calls + tracer limitations (2026-06-30)\n\nThe Phase-1 author surfaced six judgment calls (Trap 6). Ratified after review:\n\n1. **106 parks on project-link-absent, not parent-task-absent** — RATIFIED. `upsert_from_node`\n   (`tasks.rs:566`) has no parent-task FK; the real transient dependency is the ProjectsSync link, which\n   `handle_task_sync` already encodes. Correct reading of SC2b at the task tier.\n2. **106 splits PARK (transient, `node_local_projects` row absent) vs SKIP+ADVANCE (permanent,\n   not swarm-linked)** — RATIFIED, and load-bearing. Because 105 enqueues for ALL projects (the `db`\n   crate can't cheaply do the swarm lookup), a non-swarm task at the outbox head would park *permanently*\n   and wedge the cursor if \"not linked\" parked. The split (encoded as 106's third test) prevents the\n   wedge. This mirrors `handle_task_sync`'s three-branch resolution.\n3. **105 idempotency_key = `task:{id}:{uuid}` (per-write-unique, persisted on the op row), NOT\n   `task:{id}:{version}`** — RATIFIED. `Task::update` (`queries.rs:305`) bumps no version, so a\n   version-key would self-collide and `UNIQUE(idempotency_key)` would silently drop updates. A re-sent\n   op reuses its stored key → hive dedups. (Same no-version fact as ADR-0007's dirty-guard motivation.)\n4. **105 enqueue is best-effort, non-atomic** with the task write (callers hold `&SqlitePool`, not a\n   txn) — RATIFIED as a TRACER LIMITATION. The legacy sync path is the backstop. **Consequence:\n   Phase-1-tracer does NOT fully satisfy SC2c \"zero silent write loss\" — true no-loss needs the enqueue\n   in the SAME transaction as the entity write** (threading a txn through the ~8 `Task::create` callers),\n   which is the next Phase-1 increment. SC2c is *claimed* by 102/106/108 (the durable-ack mechanism) but\n   the no-loss guarantee is only fully closed by the transactional enqueue.\n5. **108 advances the cursor via a new `HiveEvent::OpAck`** consumed in `run_node_runner` (which holds\n   the pool), mirroring the `TaskSyncResponse`/`BackfillRequest` \"DB write happens in run_node_runner\"\n   pattern — RATIFIED. `HiveEvent` has no third/cross-crate match site (grep-verified), so 108's `files:`\n   (hive_client.rs + node_runner.rs) is complete.\n6. **Trap 2b (Postgres) applies to 102 + 106** — RATIFIED; each states the live-PG precondition.\n\n**Honest SC2 status after Phase-1-tracer:** the ordered, acknowledged round-trip *mechanism* is proven\n(SC2a single ordered channel — additive, alongside legacy; SC2b parent/link-before-child parking; SC2c\ndurable per-op ack + cursor-advance-only-on-ack). NOT yet done: transactional enqueue (full SC2c\nno-loss), attempt/exec/log op types, and retirement of the five legacy push paths. These are tracked as\nthe next Phase-1 increment in plan.md.\n\n## Phase-1 sibling-advisory acknowledgement (wai-plan-lint `W:` lines, SC6)\n\n- **101 `…_add_node_outbox.sql` beside `…_init.sql`** — migrations are independent forward-only DDL, NOT\n  reimplementations of a pattern. The work spans **both ends of a\n14: network protocol** and is sequenced so the **foundation flows end-to-end before anything rides it**:\n15: the ordered, acknowledged op-log (SC2) is the channel every later guarantee depends on, so it ships\n16: first as a tracer bullet — one op type flowing node→hive with a durable ack — then the remaining op\n17: types, then the mechanisms that ride it (fencing, status machine, anti-entropy). The inbound-channel\n18: collapse (SC7) and the cutover migration (SC6) are comparatively independent and ship in their own\n19: phases.\n20: \n21: Every task is Rust (or a migration/CI/frontend task). **This repo is a Cargo workspace, so the WAI\n22: gate's TypeScript type-check is skipped and its `scope_test` runner has no native `cargo test` path** —\n23: every Rust task carries explicit `WAI_TYPECHECK_CMD`/`WAI_TEST_CMD` overrides (decisions-ledger Trap 1).\n24: **SQLx is offline-mode** (committed `.sqlx` cache, `DATABASE_URL` unset): schema/query tasks execute\n25: against a live migrated dev DB and never run `cargo sqlx prepare` in a gated task (Trap 2). Adding any\n26: `NodeMessage`/`ServerMessage` WS variant (the op-log/ack/heartbeat/lease messages) hits the\n27: **enum-exhaustiveness trap on BOTH ends** (Trap 3) — every match arm in the same commit. Anchors were\n28: authored against current `main`; the adversarial breakdown tournament re-verifies each before any code.\n29: \n30: **This decompose covers the protocol + data plane (SC2–SC7 and the no-fan-out, data-plane half of\n31: SC1).** The *hive central-management web UI* half of SC1 is a carve candidate (see Scope note) decided\n32: with the user before task authoring, mirroring the node-foundations → `vk-swarm-node-ui-localize` split.\n33: \n34: Phase dependency spine: **P1 (op-log) → P2 (fencing) → P3 (status machine)**; **P1 → P5 (anti-entropy)**;\n35: **P4 (inbound collapse)** is independent of the spine; **P7 (cutover migration)** depends on the\n36: rebuilt schema (P1–P3); **P6 (no fan-out)** is data-plane and independent.\n37: \n38: ## Phases\n39: \n40: 1. **phase-1-oplog** — node→hive single ordered, acknowledged op-log/outbox: outbox table, op append on\n41:    local writes, WS stream in seq order, hive idempotent apply + durable ack, cursor-advance-on-ack,\n42:    parent-before-child parking. Replaces the five push paths (SC2). *Foundation.*\n43: 2. **phase-2-lease-fencing** — assignment via atomic checkout + lease (`lease_expires_at`), heartbeat\n44:    renewal, monotonic fencing token on grants and on op-log ops, hive stale-token rejection, node\n45:    self-fencing (reuses the ADR-0001 process fence). Discharges node-foundations D7 (SC3). Depends P1.\n46: 3. **phase-3-status-machine** — explicit `task.status` transition matrix, single-author enforcement\n47:    (hive vs node, gated on lease+token), status enum value canonicalization (SC4). Depends P1, P2.\n48: 4. **phase-4-inbound-collapse** — WS activity stream as the single live inbound channel; bulk snapshot\n49:    demoted to reconcile-only; remove the dead Electric task-shape path; one delete semantic\n50:    (soft-unlink + tombstone); node dirty-guard conflict policy; handle `task.reassigned` (SC7).\n51: 5. **phase-5-anti-entropy** — digest exchange (per-entity version/hash + outbox high-water) over the\n52:    op-log, gap heal replacing manual `reset_*` migrations (SC5). Depends P1 (+P4 reconcile leg).\n53: 6. **phase-6-no-fanout** — **verify + guard** that nodes receive only assignment/ack traffic, never\n54:    pushed shared-task state (SC1 data-plane half). Investigation found this is *already* true today —\n55:    the node-facing channel carries only `ProjectSync`/`NodeRemoved` — so phase-6 asserts and fences the\n56:    invariant against regression; it is NOT a large fan-out removal. Browser-facing shared-task fan-out\n57:    (electric_proxy/ActivityBroker) is the hive-UI data source and is OUT of scope. Depends P1, P2.\n58: 7. **phase-7-cutover** — one-time hive-only-state migration (migrate / regenerate / discard per\n59:    ADR-0011), preserving the node↔hive id bridge and remapping status enum values (SC6). Depends P1–P3.\n60: \n61: ## Scope note — SC1 central-management UI CARVED to `vk-swarm-hive-ui`\n62: \n63: SC1 has two halves: (a) the **data-plane** guarantee \"no node↔node / node↔hive↔node fan-out\" (covered\n64: here, phase-6), and (b) the **hive web UI manages all** nodes/projects/tasks/attempts/executions.\n65: **User decision (2026-06-30): half (b) is carved into `vk-swarm-hive-ui`** (tracker seeded; rehost +\n66: rewire + net-new cross-node views — see that README and the decisions ledger). This plan covers SC2–SC7\n67: + SC1's data-plane half. The work spans **both ends of a\nnetwork protocol** and is sequenced so the **foundation flows end-to-end before anything rides it**:\nthe ordered, acknowledged op-log (SC2) is the channel every later guarantee depends on, so it ships\nfirst as a tracer bullet — one op type flowing node→hive with a durable ack — then the remaining op\ntypes, then the mechanisms that ride it (fencing, status machine, anti-entropy). The inbound-channel\ncollapse (SC7) and the cutover migration (SC6) are comparatively independent and ship in their own\nphases.\n\nEvery task is Rust (or a migration/CI/frontend task). **This repo is a Cargo workspace, so the WAI\ngate's TypeScript type-check is skipped and its `scope_test` runner has no native `cargo test` path** —\nevery Rust task carries explicit `WAI_TYPECHECK_CMD`/`WAI_TEST_CMD` overrides (decisions-ledger Trap 1).\n**SQLx is offline-mode** (committed `.sqlx` cache, `DATABASE_URL` unset): schema/query tasks execute\nagainst a live migrated dev DB and never run `cargo sqlx prepare` in a gated task (Trap 2). Adding any\n`NodeMessage`/`ServerMessage` WS variant (the op-log/ack/heartbeat/lease messages) hits the\n**enum-exhaustiveness trap on BOTH ends** (Trap 3) — every match arm in the same commit. Anchors were\nauthored against current `main`; the adversarial breakdown tournament re-verifies each before any code.\n\n**This decompose covers the protocol + data plane (SC2–SC7 and the no-fan-out, data-plane half of\nSC1).** The *hive central-management web UI* half of SC1 is a carve candidate (see Scope note) decided\nwith the user before task authoring, mirroring the node-foundations → `vk-swarm-node-ui-localize` split.\n\nPhase dependency spine: **P1 (op-log) → P2 (fencing) → P3 (status machine)**; **P1 → P5 (anti-entropy)**;\n**P4 (inbound collapse)** is independent of the spine; **P7 (cutover migration)** depends on the\nrebuilt schema (P1–P3); **P6 (no fan-out)** is data-plane and independent.\n\n## Phases\n\n1. **phase-1-oplog** — node→hive single ordered, acknowledged op-log/outbox: outbox table, op append on\n   local writes, WS stream in seq order, hive idempotent apply + durable ack, cursor-advance-on-ack,\n   parent-before-child parking. Replaces the five push paths (SC2). *Foundation.*\n2. **phase-2-lease-fencing** — assignment via atomic checkout + lease (`lease_expires_at`), heartbeat\n   renewal, monotonic fencing token on grants and on op-log ops, hive stale-token rejection, node\n   self-fencing (reuses the ADR-0001 process fence). Discharges node-foundations D7 (SC3). Depends P1.\n3. **phase-3-status-machine** — explicit `task.status` transition matrix, single-author enforcement\n   (hive vs node, gated on lease+token), status enum value canonicalization (SC4). Depends P1, P2.\n4. **phase-4-inbound-collapse** — WS activity stream as the single live inbound channel; bulk snapshot\n   demoted to reconcile-only; remove the dead Electric task-shape path; one delete semantic\n   (soft-unlink + tombstone); node dirty-guard conflict policy; handle `task.reassigned` (SC7).\n5. **phase-5-anti-entropy** — digest exchange (per-entity version/hash + outbox high-water) over the\n   op-log, gap heal replacing manual `reset_*` migrations (SC5). Depends P1 (+P4 reconcile leg).\n6. **phase-6-no-fanout** — **verify + guard** that nodes receive only assignment/ack traffic, never\n   pushed shared-task state (SC1 data-plane half). Investigation found this is *already* true today —\n   the node-facing channel carries only `ProjectSync`/`NodeRemoved` — so phase-6 asserts and fences the\n   invariant against regression; it is NOT a large fan-out removal. Browser-facing shared-task fan-out\n   (electric_proxy/ActivityBroker) is the hive-UI data source and is OUT of scope. Depends P1, P2.\n7. **phase-7-cutover** — one-time hive-only-state migration (migrate / regenerate / discard per\n   ADR-0011), preserving the node↔hive id bridge and remapping status enum values (SC6). Depends P1–P3.\n\n## Scope note — SC1 central-management UI CARVED to `vk-swarm-hive-ui`\n\nSC1 has two halves: (a) the **data-plane** guarantee \"no node↔node / node↔hive↔node fan-out\" (covered\nhere, phase-6), and (b) the **hive web UI manages all** nodes/projects/tasks/attempts/executions.\n**User decision (2026-06-30): half (b) is carved into `vk-swarm-hive-ui`** (tracker seeded; rehost +\nrewire + net-new cross-node views — see that README and the decisions ledger). This plan covers SC2–SC7\n+ SC1's data-plane half. SC1 stays in the frozen spec, claimed by phase-6; no spec edit was made.\n\n## Task table\n\n`dep:`/`conflicts:` mirror each task's frontmatter (wai-plan-lint enforces equality). `-` = none.\n**Phase 1 is authored (this pass); Phases 2–7 are authored in subsequent `/wai:decompose` passes** as\neach prior ships (user-approved phase-by-phase, decisions-ledger).\n\n### Phase 1 — op-log foundation (SC2; authored as a safe additive tracer, op_type `task.upsert`)\n\n| id  | title | dep | conflicts | SC |\n|-----|-------|-----|-----------|----|\n| 101 | Add `node_outbox` table migration (SQLite) | dep: - | conflicts: none | SC2a |\n| 102 | Add `node_op_log` table migration (Postgres/hive) | dep: - | conflicts: none | SC2c |\n| 103 | Add `OpBatch`/`OutboxOp`/`OpAck` WS variants to both crates + exhaustive stub arms | dep: - | conflicts: 106 108 | SC2a |\n| 104 | Add node `OutboxRepository` (enqueue/peek_unacked/mark_acked_through) | dep: 101 | conflicts: none | SC2a |\n| 105 | Enqueue a `task.upsert` op on `Task::create`/`update` | dep: 104 | conflicts: none | SC2b |\n| 106 | Hive `handle_op_batch` — idempotent apply + park/skip + durable `OpAck` | dep: 102 103 | conflicts: 103 | SC2c |\n| 107 | Node streamer — drain `node_outbox` into `OpBatch` in `sync_once` | dep: 103 104 | conflicts: none | SC2a |\n| 108 | Node `OpAck` — advance ack cursor on durable hive ack | dep: 103 104 | conflicts: 103 | SC2c |\n\n> **Tracer honesty (recorded in the ledger):** Phase 1 proves the ordered-ack'd round-trip *mechanism*\n> alongside the legacy paths. {"type":"tool_use","timestamp":1782821222136,"sessionID":"ses_0e793c9a1ffeiLk31zpbRPWbnP","part":{"type":"tool","tool":"read","callID":"call_w3m0qvny","state":{"status":"completed","input":{"filePath":"/home/david/Code/vk-swarm/.claude/worktrees/bridge-cse_01B8B52jjMEdikaLRoA25qhr/docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-26-vk-swarm-hive-redesign.md"},"output":"<path>/home/david/Code/vk-swarm/.claude/worktrees/bridge-cse_01B8B52jjMEdikaLRoA25qhr/docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-26-vk-swarm-hive-redesign.md</path>\n<type>file</type>\n<content>\n1: ---\n2: doc_type: spec\n3: status: active\n4: workstream: vk-swarm-hive-redesign\n5: change_kind: behaviour\n6: ---\n7: \n8: # vk-swarm-hive-redesign — Rebuild the hive as a hub-and-spoke central management layer (Phase 2b)\n9: \n10: > **Child of** [`vk-swarm-refactor`](./2026-06-25-vk-swarm-refactor.md). **Depends on**\n11: > [`vk-swarm-node-foundations`](./2026-06-26-vk-swarm-node-foundations.md) — starts only after the\n12: > node works 100% standalone.\n13: >\n14: > **Analysis basis (do not duplicate):** the sync root-cause verdict and evidence live in\n15: > [`docs/specs/2026-06-25-vk-swarm-phase1-analysis.md`](../../specs/2026-06-25-vk-swarm-phase1-analysis.md)\n16: > §2 (and §2.7, redirected below). This PRD captures *intent*; `/wai:spec` designs the protocol.\n17: \n18: ## Intent (what / why)\n19: \n20: Replace the current ad-hoc **bidirectional multi-master** sync (field-level last-write-wins, two\n21: divergent inbound channels, node↔hive↔node fan-out) with a **hub-and-spoke central management layer**.\n22: Phase 1 found the sync instability is **architectural, not migration debt** (§2): a child\n23: `task_attempt` can sync before its parent `task` is linked, dirty flags clear before any Hive ack\n24: (silent write loss), and two inbound channels apply the same change with divergent semantics. The\n25: maintainers' live-data `reset_*` repair migrations are the evidence.\n26: \n27: The new model partitions authority by data type and direction:\n28: - The **hive is the central management plane**: it owns the global board and cross-node management, and\n29:   its web UI reads Postgres directly — no fan-out of shared task state to nodes.\n30: - **Nodes report up** through a single durable, ordered, acknowledged outbox; they **do not** render or\n31:   manage other nodes' state (enforced by `vk-swarm-node-foundations` SC5).\n32: - The hive **assigns work down** with lease/atomic-checkout semantics.\n33: \n34: This is the standard reliable fleet/agent control-plane shape — the same pattern as the **paperclip**\n35: reference (`/data/Code/reference/agents/paperclip`: REST heartbeat, atomic task checkout, budgets,\n36: approval gates). Topology change *eliminates the concurrent-write conflict class*; the ordering,\n37: status-ownership, and assignment-safety problems below are designed in explicitly (topology alone does\n38: not solve them).\n39: \n40: ## Users / who is affected\n41: \n42: - **The operator** — gains a single central UI to manage all nodes/projects/tasks, instead of\n43:   per-node UIs and node↔node coordination.\n44: - **Multi-node swarm users** — relieved of the §2 corruption class (no more `reset_*` repairs).\n45: - **Downstream phases (P3, P6)** — the AI breakdown harness and management agent get a single\n46:   authoritative management plane and event source to drive.\n47: \n48: ## User stories\n49: \n50: - **US1:** As the operator of a multi-node swarm, when I manage nodes/projects/tasks, I expect a single\n51:   central hive UI reading Postgres directly, with no node↔node or node↔hive↔node fan-out.\n52: - **US2:** As a multi-node swarm user, when a node writes locally over a flaky link, I expect node→hive\n53:   sync on one ordered, acknowledged channel with correct parent-before-child ordering and zero silent\n54:   write loss.\n55: - **US3:** As the operator, when the network partitions mid-run, I expect hive→node assignment to use\n56:   lease / atomic-checkout so the same task is never double-executed.\n57: - **US4:** As a swarm user, when a task moves through its lifecycle, I expect status transitions to\n58:   follow an explicit state machine with no field-level conflict.\n59: - **US5:** As the operator, when a node and the hive diverge, I expect self-healing reconciliation so I\n60:   never have to run a manual `reset_*` repair migration.\n61: - **US6:** As the operator, when we cut over to the rebuilt hive, I expect all hive-only state to be\n62:   inventoried and either migrated or explicitly handled — nothing silently lost.\n63: - **US7:** As a swarm user, when the hive delivers a change to a node, I expect one inbound channel with\n64:   one delete semantic and one conflict policy applied uniformly.\n65: \n66: ## Success criteria\n67: \n68: - SC1: The hive is the **central management plane** — its web UI manages all connected nodes,\n69:   projects, tasks, attempts, and executions, reading from Postgres directly with **no node↔node or\n70:   node↔hive↔node fan-out**. → US1\n71: - SC2: Node→hive sync uses a **single ordered, acknowledged per-node outbox/op-log** with idempotency\n72:   keys; **cross-entity ordering** (parent task before child attempt) is guaranteed by construction and\n73:   there is **zero silent write loss** (dirty state clears only after hive durable commit). *(Clauses:\n74:   SC2a ordered single channel; SC2b parent-before-child; SC2c ack'd no-loss.)* → US2\n75: - SC3: Hive→node **assignment uses lease / atomic-checkout** (heartbeat + lease expiry + idempotent\n76:   claim); a network partition **cannot cause double execution** of the same task. → US3\n77: - SC4: `task.status` transitions follow an **explicit state machine** naming which transitions are\n78:   **hive-authored** (`assigned`, `in-progress`) vs **node-reported** (`done`, `failed`); no field-level\n79:   conflict on status. → US4\n80: - SC5: Node↔hive divergence **self-heals** via an anti-entropy reconciliation sweep — **no manual\n81:   `reset_*` migration** is ever required. → US5\n82: - SC6: A **migration inventory** of all state that lives *only* in the hive today (cross-node\n83:   assignments, board organization, manual hive-UI edits) is complete, and that state is migrated or\n84:   explicitly handled on cutover to the rebuilt hive. → US6\n85: - SC7: The two live inbound channels (REST bulk-snapshot reconcile + WS activity stream) are\n86:   **collapsed to one**, with **one delete semantic and one conflict policy** applied uniformly. (The\n87:   Electric SQL `shared_tasks` shape poll named in analysis §2.3 is **dead in code** — no Rust caller;\n88:   it is removed, not collapsed.) → US7\n89: \n90: ## Constraints\n91: \n92: - **Keep:** Postgres as the hive store, WebSocket transport, local SQLite as node-of-record. Rebuild\n93:   the *reconciliation contract and management surface*, not the storage engines.\n94: - **Start only after `vk-swarm-node-foundations` is complete** — the rebuilt hive re-ingests\n95:   node-authoritative state via the new outbox; nodes must be the reliable source first.\n96: - **Resolve the redirected §2.7 check before the cutover design hardens:** the open question is no\n97:   longer \"targeted vs rebuild\" (rebuild is chosen) but the **migration inventory** (SC6) plus the\n98:   broadcast-fan-out and SQLite↔Postgres schema-drift checks.\n99: - **Nodes manage local-only;** the central management surface lives here, not on nodes\n100:   (`vk-swarm-node-foundations` SC5 is the enforcing boundary).\n101: - **GitHub targeting:** PRs only against `davidrudduck/vk-swarm`.\n102: \n103: ## Out of scope\n104: \n105: - **Node-local durability and crash-resumability** — owned by `vk-swarm-node-foundations`.\n106: - **Hive HA / replication** — a named *future* requirement (every node retains its always-on local UI\n107:   as the management fallback during a hive outage); not in this workstream.\n108: - **Schema/migration consolidation** beyond what the rebuild requires — hygiene, deferred.\n109: - **P3+ AI breakdown / event bus / management agent** — consumers of this plane, designed later.\n110: \n111: ## Approach\n112: \n113: Rebuild the **reconciliation contract and management surface** as a hub-and-spoke control plane while\n114: keeping the storage engines (Postgres hive store, SQLite node-of-record, WS transport — per\n115: Constraints). The rebuild itself is settled at program level (analysis §2.6); this design fixes the four\n116: defect classes Phase 1 proved by collapsing channels and adding the guarantees topology alone does not\n117: give. The three §2.7 open items were **resolved in code** (read-only investigation, cited below), as the\n118: Constraints require before the cutover design hardens:\n119: \n120: - **Cross-entity ordering is already declaratively enforced** (`hive_sync.rs:340-349` skip-when-unlinked\n121:   + JOIN guards `execution_process/sync.rs:22-23`, `log_entry/sync.rs:26-27`) — *guardable*, so the\n122:   op-log preserves it by construction rather than re-deriving it. The real defect is **ack timing**\n123:   (flags clear on mpsc-enqueue, not durable ack → silent write loss).\n124: - **The two inbound channels can double-deliver and diverge on delete** (one hive tx writes\n125:   `shared_tasks` + an activity row, `remote/src/db/tasks.rs:892-893`; bulk-snapshot **hard-deletes**\n126:   vs WS activity **soft-unlinks**), and `task.reassigned` is dropped by the activity processor\n127:   (`processor.rs:77`). The live second channel is the **REST bulk-snapshot reconcile**\n128:   (`node_runner.rs:986`); the Electric `shared_tasks` shape path is **dead** (no Rust caller; frontend\n129:   subscribes only to `nodes`/`projects` shapes) — SC7's parenthetical was corrected to reflect this.\n130: - **`tasks` column drift is moderate-high**, with a load-bearing **status enum value mismatch**\n131:   (`inprogress`/`inreview` vs hyphenated `in-progress`/`in-review`) and **two distinct id spaces**\n132:   bridged by `shared_task_id` ↔ `source_task_id`.\n133: \n134: The **node-side outbox writer and the heartbeat/fencing client are new work introduced here** —\n135: `vk-swarm-node-foundations` deliberately left the node↔hive sync *contract* out of scope (its SC5 only\n136: stripped the node UI; sync plumbing was left intact). This workstream owns both ends of the contract.\n137: \n138: ## Design / architecture\n139: \n140: Each mechanism maps 1:1 to a success criterion and a backing ADR.\n141: \n142: **1. Hive as central management plane, zero fan-out (SC1).** The hive web UI manages all\n143: nodes/projects/tasks/attempts/executions reading Postgres directly. Hive→node traffic is **only\n144: assignments and acks directed at that node** — never a replica of the global board pushed to every\n145: node. The node→node and node↔hive↔node fan-out paths (`remote/src/activity/broker.rs` broadcast) are\n146: removed for shared task state. This dissolves the §2 concurrent-write conflict class at the topology\n147: level (inherited program decision; analysis §2.6).\n148: \n149: **2. Single ordered, acknowledged outbox / op-log (SC2 · [ADR-0008](../../../dev-docs/adr/0008-node-hive-ordered-ack-outbox.md)).**\n150: Replace the five node→hive push paths (`hive_sync.rs:303/368/434/562`, `share/publisher.rs:109`) with\n151: one per-node append-only `outbox(seq, op_type, entity_type, entity_id, payload, idempotency_key,\n152: fencing_token, acked_at)` in node SQLite. Ops stream in `seq` order over the WS; the hive applies\n153: idempotently (`idempotency_key` UNIQUE + `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`), **parks a child op until its parent\n154: applies** (SC2b), and returns a **durable ack** carrying the applied high-water `seq`. The node clears\n155: `acked_at`/advances its cursor **only on durable ack** (SC2c) — closing the silent-loss window. Per-op\n156: monotonic version replaces the hardcoded `version: 1` (`hive_sync.rs:289`).\n157: \n158: **3. Lease / atomic-checkout assignment, partition-safe via fencing (SC3 · [ADR-0009](../../../dev-docs/adr/0009-lease-checkout-fencing.md)).**\n159: The hive assigns by atomic CAS (`UPDATE node_task_assignments … WHERE <available> RETURNING`) — no two\n160: nodes both claim. Each grant carries `lease_expires_at` + a monotonic **fencing token**; the node\n161: renews via heartbeat. On missed renewal the hive reclaims with a **higher** token. **Fencing is scoped\n162: to hive-assigned tasks:** the node stamps every outbox op **against a hive-assigned task** with that\n163: task's current lease token, and the hive **rejects stale-token commits** on assigned tasks →\n164: **at-most-once commit effect**. Node-owned work (locally-created tasks and their attempts/execs/logs —\n165: the majority of outbox traffic) carries **no lease token** and is committed under the node's ownership\n166: identity, not a lease. The node **self-fences** (halts the agent via ADR-0001's process-group kill) when\n167: it cannot renew → **bounded execution overlap**. Together: a partition cannot cause double-execution\n168: *effect*. This **discharges node-foundations D7** (foreign-row disambiguation).\n169: \n170: **4. Explicit `task.status` state machine (SC4 · [ADR-0010](../../../dev-docs/adr/0010-task-status-state-machine.md)).**\n171: A guarded transition matrix with one authoritative author per transition: **hive-authored**\n172: `todo→assigned`, `assigned→in-progress`, `*→cancelled`; **node-reported** `in-progress→done`,\n173: `in-progress→failed` (accepted only with a valid lease + fencing token). No field-level status merge.\n174: One canonical wire value resolves the `inprogress`/`in-progress` drift.\n175: \n176: **5. Anti-entropy reconciliation (SC5 · [ADR-0008](../../../dev-docs/adr/0008-node-hive-ordered-ack-outbox.md)).**\n177: Riding the op-log: on reconnect and periodically the node re-streams from its unacked cursor, and a\n178: **digest exchange** (per-entity version/hash + outbox high-water) detects silent divergence the cursor\n179: misses; the hive replies with the ops/pulls to heal. The repurposed bulk-snapshot reconcile\n180: ([ADR-0007](../../../dev-docs/adr/0007-single-inbound-channel-one-delete-one-conflict.md)) is its\n181: gap-fill leg. This *replaces* the manual `reset_*` repair migrations.\n182: \n183: **6. Hive-only-state cutover inventory (SC6 · [ADR-0011](../../../dev-docs/adr/0011-hive-only-state-cutover.md)).**\n184: The redirected §2.7. Full read-only inventory classifies every hive-only table as **must-migrate**\n185: (`node_api_keys`, `nodes`, active `node_task_assignments`, `swarm_projects`/`swarm_project_nodes`,\n186: `swarm_templates`, `shared_tasks` incl. attribution + the id bridge, `labels`/`shared_task_labels`,\n187: identity/tenancy), **regenerable** (node-mirror caches/logs/sync bookkeeping — rebuilt by node\n188: re-ingest), or **discardable** (activity history, sessions, completed assignments). **No board-ordering\n189: table exists** (order derived from `status`+`activity_at`) — no layout to migrate. Cutover: run the\n190: must-migrate migration preserving the id bridge, then nodes reconnect and re-ingest regenerable state.\n191: \n192: **7. Single inbound channel, one delete, one conflict (SC7 · [ADR-0007](../../../dev-docs/adr/0007-single-inbound-channel-one-delete-one-conflict.md)).**\n193: WS activity stream becomes the single live inbound channel; the bulk snapshot is demoted to\n194: cold-start/gap-fill reconcile; the dead Electric task-shape path is removed. One delete semantic\n195: (hive soft-delete → node **soft-unlink + tombstone**, preserving local attempts) applied identically on\n196: both legs. One conflict policy: hive authoritative + node **dirty-guard** (an inbound update never\n197: overwrites a field with an unacked outbound op) — replacing the `remote_version`-only gate that silently\n198: clobbers local edits (`task/sync.rs:300`, `task/queries.rs:305-307`). The single channel handles\n199: `task.reassigned`.\n200: \n201: ## Decisions\n202: \n203: - **D1 — Collapse hive→node delivery to one live channel (WS activity), reconcile-only bulk snapshot,\n204:   delete the dead Electric task path; one delete semantic + one conflict policy.** *(Irreversible:\n205:   wire-format + code delete + delete-semantic change.)* → [ADR-0007](../../../dev-docs/adr/0007-single-inbound-channel-one-delete-one-conflict.md)\n206: - **D2 — Replace the five node→hive push paths with one ordered, ack'd per-node op-log/outbox**;\n207:   cursor advances only on durable ack; parent-before-child by construction; anti-entropy digest rides\n208:   it (SC5). *(Irreversible: wire format + deletes legacy push code.)* → [ADR-0008](../../../dev-docs/adr/0008-node-hive-ordered-ack-outbox.md)\n209: - **D3 — Assignment = atomic checkout + lease, made partition-safe by fencing tokens + node\n210:   self-fencing** (at-most-once effect, bounded overlap); **discharges node-foundations D7**.\n211:   *(Irreversible: assignment contract + fencing-token wire field.)* → [ADR-0009](../../../dev-docs/adr/0009-lease-checkout-fencing.md)\n212: - **D4 — `task.status` is an explicit single-author transition matrix**; one canonical status wire\n213:   value (resolve `inprogress`/`in-progress` drift). *(Irreversible: contract + enum value\n214:   canonicalization.)* → [ADR-0010](../../../dev-docs/adr/0010-task-status-state-machine.md)\n215: - **D5 — Hive-only state cutover** → [ADR-0011](../../../dev-docs/adr/0011-hive-only-state-cutover.md) *(Irreversible: data migration / drop)*. Classified migrate /\n216:   regenerate / discard with a pre-cutover backup; the node↔hive id bridge is preserved; no\n217:   board-ordering table to migrate.\n218: - **D6 — The node-side outbox writer + heartbeat/fencing client are new work owned here** (not by\n219:   `vk-swarm-node-foundations`, which left sync plumbing intact). *(Reversible scope note.)*\n220: - **D7 — SC7's parenthetical was corrected** from \"Electric SQL shape poll\" to \"REST bulk-snapshot\n221:   reconcile\" — a factual fix (the Electric task path is dead in code), not an intent change; the\n222:   collapse-two-to-one criterion is unchanged. *(Reversible doc correction.)*\n223: \n224: ## Test strategy\n225: \n226: - **TS1: Ordered ack'd outbox, no silent loss (SC2).** With the `qa_mock` executor and a fault-injected\n227:   WS, drop the connection between op-enqueue and hive ack; assert the op is **retried** (not cleared)\n228:   and applies exactly once (idempotency key); assert a child op is **parked** until its parent applies.\n229:   Use `db::test_utils::create_test_pool()` for the node side.\n230: - **TS2: Partition cannot double-execute (SC3).** Lease a task to node A; simulate A partitioned but\n231:   alive; expire + reassign to B (higher fencing token); assert A's late commit is **rejected by\n232:   stale-token** and A **self-fences** (agent halted) within TTL — at-most-once effect, bounded overlap.\n233: - **TS3: status state machine (SC4).** Table-driven over the transition matrix: each legal transition is\n234:   accepted from its sole author and **rejected** from the other party / without a valid lease+token;\n235:   assert the `inprogress`↔`in-progress` value maps to one canonical wire form.\n236: - **TS4: anti-entropy self-heal (SC5).** Seed a divergence (node has an entity the hive lacks and vice\n237:   versa); run the digest-exchange sweep; assert convergence with **no `reset_*`-style manual step**.\n238: - **TS5: single inbound channel semantics (SC7).** Assert a hive soft-delete yields **one** node\n239:   outcome (soft-unlink + tombstone, local attempt retained) regardless of leg; assert a concurrent\n240:   local edit is **not** clobbered by an inbound update (dirty-guard); assert `task.reassigned` is\n241:   applied on the single channel.\n242: - **TS6: cutover inventory (SC6).** A migration test asserts every **must-migrate** table round-trips\n243:   into the rebuilt schema with the id bridge intact and status values remapped; **regenerable** tables\n244:   repopulate from a simulated node re-ingest; **discardable** tables are absent — nothing in the\n245:   inventory is silently lost.\n246: - **TS7: no fan-out (SC1).** Assert a task owned by node X is **not** pushed to node Y; node Y's inbound\n247:   stream contains only its own assignments/acks (topology check).\n\n(End of file - total 247 lines)\n</content>","metadata":{"preview":"---\ndoc_type: spec\nstatus: active\nworkstream: vk-swarm-hive-redesign\nchange_kind: behaviour\n---\n\n# vk-swarm-hive-redesign — Rebuild the hive as a hub-and-spoke central management layer (Phase 2b)\n\n> **Child of** [`vk-swarm-refactor`](./2026-06-25-vk-swarm-refactor.md). **Depends on**\n> [`vk-swarm-node-foundations`](./2026-06-26-vk-swarm-node-foundations.md) — starts only after the\n> node works 100% standalone.\n>\n> **Analysis basis (do not duplicate):** the sync root-cause verdict and evidence live in\n> [`docs/specs/2026-06-25-vk-swarm-phase1-analysis.md`](../../specs/2026-06-25-vk-swarm-phase1-analysis.md)\n> §2 (and §2.7, redirected below). This PRD captures *intent*; `/wai:spec` designs the protocol.\n\n## Intent (what / why)\n\nReplace the current ad-hoc **bidirectional multi-master** sync (field-level last-write-wins, two","truncated":false,"loaded":[],"display":{"type":"file","path":"/home/david/Code/vk-swarm/.claude/worktrees/bridge-cse_01B8B52jjMEdikaLRoA25qhr/docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-26-vk-swarm-hive-redesign.md","text":"---\ndoc_type: spec\nstatus: active\nworkstream: vk-swarm-hive-redesign\nchange_kind: behaviour\n---\n\n# vk-swarm-hive-redesign — Rebuild the hive as a hub-and-spoke central management layer (Phase 2b)\n\n> **Child of** [`vk-swarm-refactor`](./2026-06-25-vk-swarm-refactor.md). **Depends on**\n> [`vk-swarm-node-foundations`](./2026-06-26-vk-swarm-node-foundations.md) — starts only after the\n> node works 100% standalone.\n>\n> **Analysis basis (do not duplicate):** the sync root-cause verdict and evidence live in\n> [`docs/specs/2026-06-25-vk-swarm-phase1-analysis.md`](../../specs/2026-06-25-vk-swarm-phase1-analysis.md)\n> §2 (and §2.7, redirected below). This PRD captures *intent*; `/wai:spec` designs the protocol.\n\n## Intent (what / why)\n\nReplace the current ad-hoc **bidirectional multi-master** sync (field-level last-write-wins, two\ndivergent inbound channels, node↔hive↔node fan-out) with a **hub-and-spoke central management layer**.\nPhase 1 found the sync instability is **architectural, not migration debt** (§2): a child\n`task_attempt` can sync before its parent `task` is linked, dirty flags clear before any Hive ack\n(silent write loss), and two inbound channels apply the same change with divergent semantics. The\nmaintainers' live-data `reset_*` repair migrations are the evidence.\n\nThe new model partitions authority by data type and direction:\n- The **hive is the central management plane**: it owns the global board and cross-node management, and\n  its web UI reads Postgres directly — no fan-out of shared task state to nodes.\n- **Nodes report up** through a single durable, ordered, acknowledged outbox; they **do not** render or\n  manage other nodes' state (enforced by `vk-swarm-node-foundations` SC5).\n- The hive **assigns work down** with lease/atomic-checkout semantics.\n\nThis is the standard reliable fleet/agent control-plane shape — the same pattern as the **paperclip**\nreference (`/data/Code/reference/agents/paperclip`: REST heartbeat, atomic task checkout, budgets,\napproval gates). Topology change *eliminates the concurrent-write conflict class*; the ordering,\nstatus-ownership, and assignment-safety problems below are designed in explicitly (topology alone does\nnot solve them).\n\n## Users / who is affected\n\n- **The operator** — gains a single central UI to manage all nodes/projects/tasks, instead of\n  per-node UIs and node↔node coordination.\n- **Multi-node swarm users** — relieved of the §2 corruption class (no more `reset_*` repairs).\n- **Downstream phases (P3, P6)** — the AI breakdown harness and management agent get a single\n  authoritative management plane and event source to drive.\n\n## User stories\n\n- **US1:** As the operator of a multi-node swarm, when I manage nodes/projects/tasks, I expect a single\n  central hive UI reading Postgres directly, with no node↔node or node↔hive↔node fan-out.\n- **US2:** As a multi-node swarm user, when a node writes locally over a flaky link, I expect node→hive\n  sync on one ordered, acknowledged channel with correct parent-before-child ordering and zero silent\n  write loss.\n- **US3:** As the operator, when the network partitions mid-run, I expect hive→node assignment to use\n  lease / atomic-checkout so the same task is never double-executed.\n- **US4:** As a swarm user, when a task moves through its lifecycle, I expect status transitions to\n  follow an explicit state machine with no field-level conflict.\n- **US5:** As the operator, when a node and the hive diverge, I expect self-healing reconciliation so I\n  never have to run a manual `reset_*` repair migration.\n- **US6:** As the operator, when we cut over to the rebuilt hive, I expect all hive-only state to be\n  inventoried and either migrated or explicitly handled — nothing silently lost.\n- **US7:** As a swarm user, when the hive delivers a change to a node, I expect one inbound channel with\n  one delete semantic and one conflict policy applied uniformly.\n\n## Success criteria\n\n- SC1: The hive is the **central management plane** — its web UI manages all connected nodes,\n  projects, tasks, attempts, and executions, reading from Postgres directly with **no node↔node or\n  node↔hive↔node fan-out**. → US1\n- SC2: Node→hive sync uses a **single ordered, acknowledged per-node outbox/op-log** with idempotency\n  keys; **cross-entity ordering** (parent task before child attempt) is guaranteed by construction and\n  there is **zero silent write loss** (dirty state clears only after hive durable commit). *(Clauses:\n  SC2a ordered single channel; SC2b parent-before-child; SC2c ack'd no-loss.)* → US2\n- SC3: Hive→node **assignment uses lease / atomic-checkout** (heartbeat + lease expiry + idempotent\n  claim); a network partition **cannot cause double execution** of the same task. → US3\n- SC4: `task.status` transitions follow an **explicit state machine** naming which transitions are\n  **hive-authored** (`assigned`, `in-progress`) vs **node-reported** (`done`, `failed`); no field-level\n  conflict on status. → US4\n- SC5: Node↔hive divergence **self-heals** via an anti-entropy reconciliation sweep — **no manual\n  `reset_*` migration** is ever required. → US5\n- SC6: A **migration inventory** of all state that lives *only* in the hive today (cross-node\n  assignments, board organization, manual hive-UI edits) is complete, and that state is migrated or\n  explicitly handled on cutover to the rebuilt hive. → US6\n- SC7: The two live inbound channels (REST bulk-snapshot reconcile + WS activity stream) are\n  **collapsed to one**, with **one delete semantic and one conflict policy** applied uniformly. (The\n  Electric SQL `shared_tasks` shape poll named in analysis §2.3 is **dead in code** — no Rust caller;\n  it is removed, not collapsed.) → US7\n\n## Constraints\n\n- **Keep:** Postgres as the hive store, WebSocket transport, local SQLite as node-of-record. Rebuild\n  the *reconciliation contract and management surface*, not the storage engines.\n- **Start only after `vk-swarm-node-foundations` is complete** — the rebuilt hive re-ingests\n  node-authoritative state via the new outbox; nodes must be the reliable source first.\n- **Resolve the redirected §2.7 check before the cutover design hardens:** the open question is no\n  longer \"targeted vs rebuild\" (rebuild is chosen) but the **migration inventory** (SC6) plus the\n  broadcast-fan-out and SQLite↔Postgres schema-drift checks.\n- **Nodes manage local-only;** the central management surface lives here, not on nodes\n  (`vk-swarm-node-foundations` SC5 is the enforcing boundary).\n- **GitHub targeting:** PRs only against `davidrudduck/vk-swarm`.\n\n## Out of scope\n\n- **Node-local durability and crash-resumability** — owned by `vk-swarm-node-foundations`.\n- **Hive HA / replication** — a named *future* requirement (every node retains its always-on local UI\n  as the management fallback during a hive outage); not in this workstream.\n- **Schema/migration consolidation** beyond what the rebuild requires — hygiene, deferred.\n- **P3+ AI breakdown / event bus / management agent** — consumers of this plane, designed later.\n\n## Approach\n\nRebuild the **reconciliation contract and management surface** as a hub-and-spoke control plane while\nkeeping the storage engines (Postgres hive store, SQLite node-of-record, WS transport — per\nConstraints). The rebuild itself is settled at program level (analysis §2.6); this design fixes the four\ndefect classes Phase 1 proved by collapsing channels and adding the guarantees topology alone does not\ngive. The three §2.7 open items were **resolved in code** (read-only investigation, cited below), as the\nConstraints require before the cutover design hardens:\n\n- **Cross-entity ordering is already declaratively enforced** (`hive_sync.rs:340-349` skip-when-unlinked\n  + JOIN guards `execution_process/sync.rs:22-23`, `log_entry/sync.rs:26-27`) — *guardable*, so the\n  op-log preserves it by construction rather than re-deriving it. The real defect is **ack timing**\n  (flags clear on mpsc-enqueue, not durable ack → silent write loss).\n- **The two inbound channels can double-deliver and diverge on delete** (one hive tx writes\n  `shared_tasks` + an activity row, `remote/src/db/tasks.rs:892-893`; bulk-snapshot **hard-deletes**\n  vs WS activity **soft-unlinks**), and `task.reassigned` is dropped by the activity processor\n  (`processor.rs:77`). The live second channel is the **REST bulk-snapshot reconcile**\n  (`node_runner.rs:986`); the Electric `shared_tasks` shape path is **dead** (no Rust caller; frontend\n  subscribes only to `nodes`/`projects` shapes) — SC7's parenthetical was corrected to reflect this.\n- **`tasks` column drift is moderate-high**, with a load-bearing **status enum value mismatch**\n  (`inprogress`/`inreview` vs hyphenated `in-progress`/`in-review`) and **two distinct id spaces**\n  bridged by `shared_task_id` ↔ `source_task_id`.\n\nThe **node-side outbox writer and the heartbeat/fencing client are new work introduced here** —\n`vk-swarm-node-foundations` deliberately left the node↔hive sync *contract* out of scope (its SC5 only\nstripped the node UI; sync plumbing was left intact). This workstream owns both ends of the contract.\n\n## Design / architecture\n\nEach mechanism maps 1:1 to a success criterion and a backing ADR.\n\n**1. Hive as central management plane, zero fan-out (SC1).** The hive web UI manages all\nnodes/projects/tasks/attempts/executions reading Postgres directly. Hive→node traffic is **only\nassignments and acks directed at that node** — never a replica of the global board pushed to every\nnode. The node→node and node↔hive↔node fan-out paths (`remote/src/activity/broker.rs` broadcast) are\nremoved for shared task state. This dissolves the §2 concurrent-write conflict class at the topology\nlevel (inherited program decision; analysis §2.6).\n\n**2. Single ordered, acknowledged outbox / op-log (SC2 · [ADR-0008](../../../dev-docs/adr/0008-node-hive-ordered-ack-outbox.md)).**\nReplace the five node→hive push paths (`hive_sync.rs:303/368/434/562`, `share/publisher.rs:109`) with\none per-node append-only `outbox(seq, op_type, entity_type, entity_id, payload, idempotency_key,\nfencing_token, acked_at)` in node SQLite. Ops stream in `seq` order over the WS; the hive applies\nidempotently (`idempotency_key` UNIQUE + `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`), **parks a child op until its parent\napplies** (SC2b), and returns a **durable ack** carrying the applied high-water `seq`. The node clears\n`acked_at`/advances its cursor **only on durable ack** (SC2c) — closing the silent-loss window. Per-op\nmonotonic version replaces the hardcoded `version: 1` (`hive_sync.rs:289`).\n\n**3. Lease / atomic-checkout assignment, partition-safe via fencing (SC3 · [ADR-0009](../../../dev-docs/adr/0009-lease-checkout-fencing.md)).**\nThe hive assigns by atomic CAS (`UPDATE node_task_assignments … WHERE <available> RETURNING`) — no two\nnodes both claim. Each grant carries `lease_expires_at` + a monotonic **fencing token**; the node\nrenews via heartbeat. On missed renewal the hive reclaims with a **higher** token. **Fencing is scoped\nto hive-assigned tasks:** the node stamps every outbox op **against a hive-assigned task** with that\ntask's current lease token, and the hive **rejects stale-token commits** on assigned tasks →\n**at-most-once commit effect**. Node-owned work (locally-created tasks and their attempts/execs/logs —\nthe majority of outbox traffic) carries **no lease token** and is committed under the node's ownership\nidentity, not a lease. The node **self-fences** (halts the agent via ADR-0001's process-group kill) when\nit cannot renew → **bounded execution overlap**. Together: a partition cannot cause double-execution\n*effect*. This **discharges node-foundations D7** (foreign-row disambiguation).\n\n**4. Explicit `task.status` state machine (SC4 · [ADR-0010](../../../dev-docs/adr/0010-task-status-state-machine.md)).**\nA guarded transition matrix with one authoritative author per transition: **hive-authored**\n`todo→assigned`, `assigned→in-progress`, `*→cancelled`; **node-reported** `in-progress→done`,\n`in-progress→failed` (accepted only with a valid lease + fencing token). No field-level status merge.\nOne canonical wire value resolves the `inprogress`/`in-progress` drift.\n\n**5. Anti-entropy reconciliation (SC5 · [ADR-0008](../../../dev-docs/adr/0008-node-hive-ordered-ack-outbox.md)).**\nRiding the op-log: on reconnect and periodically the node re-streams from its unacked cursor, and a\n**digest exchange** (per-entity version/hash + outbox high-water) detects silent divergence the cursor\nmisses; the hive replies with the ops/pulls to heal. The repurposed bulk-snapshot reconcile\n([ADR-0007](../../../dev-docs/adr/0007-single-inbound-channel-one-delete-one-conflict.md)) is its\ngap-fill leg. This *replaces* the manual `reset_*` repair migrations.\n\n**6. Hive-only-state cutover inventory (SC6 · [ADR-0011](../../../dev-docs/adr/0011-hive-only-state-cutover.md)).**\nThe redirected §2.7. Full read-only inventory classifies every hive-only table as **must-migrate**\n(`node_api_keys`, `nodes`, active `node_task_assignments`, `swarm_projects`/`swarm_project_nodes`,\n`swarm_templates`, `shared_tasks` incl. attribution + the id bridge, `labels`/`shared_task_labels`,\nidentity/tenancy), **regenerable** (node-mirror caches/logs/sync bookkeeping — rebuilt by node\nre-ingest), or **discardable** (activity history, sessions, completed assignments). **No board-ordering\ntable exists** (order derived from `status`+`activity_at`) — no layout to migrate. Cutover: run the\nmust-migrate migration preserving the id bridge, then nodes reconnect and re-ingest regenerable state.\n\n**7. Single inbound channel, one delete, one conflict (SC7 · [ADR-0007](../../../dev-docs/adr/0007-single-inbound-channel-one-delete-one-conflict.md)).**\nWS activity stream becomes the single live inbound channel; the bulk snapshot is demoted to\ncold-start/gap-fill reconcile; the dead Electric task-shape path is removed. One delete semantic\n(hive soft-delete → node **soft-unlink + tombstone**, preserving local attempts) applied identically on\nboth legs. One conflict policy: hive authoritative + node **dirty-guard** (an inbound update never\noverwrites a field with an unacked outbound op) — replacing the `remote_version`-only gate that silently\nclobbers local edits (`task/sync.rs:300`, `task/queries.rs:305-307`). The single channel handles\n`task.reassigned`.\n\n## Decisions\n\n- **D1 — Collapse hive→node delivery to one live channel (WS activity), reconcile-only bulk snapshot,\n  delete the dead Electric task path; one delete semantic + one conflict policy.** *(Irreversible:\n  wire-format + code delete + delete-semantic change.)* → [ADR-0007](../../../dev-docs/adr/0007-single-inbound-channel-one-delete-one-conflict.md)\n- **D2 — Replace the five node→hive push paths with one ordered, ack'd per-node op-log/outbox**;\n  cursor advances only on durable ack; parent-before-child by construction; anti-entropy digest rides\n  it (SC5). *(Irreversible: wire format + deletes legacy push code.)* → [ADR-0008](../../../dev-docs/adr/0008-node-hive-ordered-ack-outbox.md)\n- **D3 — Assignment = atomic checkout + lease, made partition-safe by fencing tokens + node\n  self-fencing** (at-most-once effect, bounded overlap); **discharges node-foundations D7**.\n  *(Irreversible: assignment contract + fencing-token wire field.)* → [ADR-0009](../../../dev-docs/adr/0009-lease-checkout-fencing.md)\n- **D4 — `task.status` is an explicit single-author transition matrix**; one canonical status wire\n  value (resolve `inprogress`/`in-progress` drift). *(Irreversible: contract + enum value\n  canonicalization.)* → [ADR-0010](../../../dev-docs/adr/0010-task-status-state-machine.md)\n- **D5 — Hive-only state cutover** → [ADR-0011](../../../dev-docs/adr/0011-hive-only-state-cutover.md) *(Irreversible: data migration / drop)*. Classified migrate /\n  regenerate / discard with a pre-cutover backup; the node↔hive id bridge is preserved; no\n  board-ordering table to migrate.\n- **D6 — The node-side outbox writer + heartbeat/fencing client are new work owned here** (not by\n  `vk-swarm-node-foundations`, which left sync plumbing intact). *(Reversible scope note.)*\n- **D7 — SC7's parenthetical was corrected** from \"Electric SQL shape poll\" to \"REST bulk-snapshot\n  reconcile\" — a factual fix (the Electric task path is dead in code), not an intent change; the\n  collapse-two-to-one criterion is unchanged. *(Reversible doc correction.)*\n\n## Test strategy\n\n- **TS1: Ordered ack'd outbox, no silent loss (SC2).** With the `qa_mock` executor and a fault-injected\n  WS, drop the connection between op-enqueue and hive ack; assert the op is **retried** (not cleared)\n  and applies exactly once (idempotency key); assert a child op is **parked** until its parent applies.\n  Use `db::test_utils::create_test_pool()` for the node side.\n- **TS2: Partition cannot double-execute (SC3).** Lease a task to node A; simulate A partitioned but\n  alive; expire + reassign to B (higher fencing token); assert A's late commit is **rejected by\n  stale-token** and A **self-fences** (agent halted) within TTL — at-most-once effect, bounded overlap.\n- **TS3: status state machine (SC4).** Table-driven over the transition matrix: each legal transition is\n  accepted from its sole author and **rejected** from the other party / without a valid lease+token;\n  assert the `inprogress`↔`in-progress` value maps to one canonical wire form.\n- **TS4: anti-entropy self-heal (SC5).** Seed a divergence (node has an entity the hive lacks and vice\n  versa); run the digest-exchange sweep; assert convergence with **no `reset_*`-style manual step**.\n- **TS5: single inbound channel semantics (SC7).** Assert a hive soft-delete yields **one** node\n  outcome (soft-unlink + tombstone, local attempt retained) regardless of leg; assert a concurrent\n  local edit is **not** clobbered by an inbound update (dirty-guard); assert `task.reassigned` is\n  applied on the single channel.\n- **TS6: cutover inventory (SC6).** A migration test asserts every **must-migrate** table round-trips\n  into the rebuilt schema with the id bridge intact and status values remapped; **regenerable** tables\n  repopulate from a simulated node re-ingest; **discardable** tables are absent — nothing in the\n  inventory is silently lost.\n- **TS7: no fan-out (SC1).** Assert a task owned by node X is **not** pushed to node Y; node Y's inbound\n  stream contains only its own assignments/acks (topology check).","lineStart":1,"lineEnd":247,"totalLines":247,"truncated":false}},"title":"docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-26-vk-swarm-hive-redesign.md","time":{"start":1782821222129,"end":1782821222134}},"id":"prt_f186cf6ec001Nonzdxj0eLrIAj","sessionID":"ses_0e793c9a1ffeiLk31zpbRPWbnP","messageID":"msg_f186c9515002X9Ljluw8L60Duw"}}

fencing_token: None,\n        };\n\n        let a = OutboxRepository::enqueue_op(&pool, mk(\"task:a:1\")).await.unwrap();\n        let b = OutboxRepository::enqueue_op(&pool, mk(\"task:b:1\")).await.unwrap();\n        assert!(b.seq > a.seq, \"seq must be per-node monotonic\");\n\n        let unacked = OutboxRepository::peek_unacked(&pool, 10).await.unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(unacked.len(), 2);\n        assert_eq!(unacked[0].seq, a.seq, \"peek_unacked is seq-ordered\");\n        assert_eq!(unacked[1].seq, b.seq);\n\n        // Ack through the first op's seq → only b remains unacked.\n        OutboxRepository::mark_acked_through(&pool, a.seq).await.unwrap();\n        let remaining = OutboxRepository::peek_unacked(&pool, 10).await.unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(remaining.len(), 1);\n        assert_eq!(remaining[0].seq, b.seq);\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn enqueue_op_rejects_duplicate_idempotency_key() {\n        let (pool, _tmp) = db::test_utils::create_test_pool().await;\n        let op = NewOutboxOp {\n            op_type: \"task.upsert\".into(), entity_type: \"task\".into(),\n            entity_id: uuid::Uuid::new_v4(), payload: serde_json::json!({}),\n            idempotency_key: \"task:dup:1\".into(), fencing_token: None,\n        };\n        OutboxRepository::enqueue_op(&pool, op.clone()).await.unwrap();\n        assert!(OutboxRepository::enqueue_op(&pool, op).await.is_err(),\n            \"UNIQUE(idempotency_key) must reject a re-enqueue\");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Change\n- **File:** Best-effort:\n140:     /// a failed enqueue is logged, NOT propagated — the legacy path remains the backstop, and the\n141:     /// enqueue is a separate statement from the task write (not one txn), so a crash between them is\n142:     /// covered by the legacy sync. (Threading a shared txn through all Task::create callers is OUT of\n143:     /// scope for the tracer — see decisions-ledger.)\n144:     async fn enqueue_task_upsert_op(pool: &SqlitePool, task: &Task) {\n145:         use crate::models::node_outbox::{NewOutboxOp, OutboxRepository};\n146:         let payload = match serde_json::to_value(task) {\n147:             Ok(v) => v,\n148:             Err(e) => { tracing::warn!(error = %e, task_id = %task.id, \"skip outbox enqueue: serialize failed\"); return; }\n149:         };\n150:         // Per-write-unique idempotency key. DELIBERATELY NOT `task:{id}:{version}`: Task::update does\n151:         // NOT bump any version column (queries.rs UPDATE sets only title/description/status/parent_task_id),\n152:         // so a version-only key collides on every update and the UNIQUE(idempotency_key) constraint\n153:         // would silently drop the update op. A fresh Uuid suffix is assigned ONCE here and persisted\n154:         // with the row, so a re-transmit of the SAME outbox row reuses the SAME key and the hive dedups\n155:         // (node_op_log PK). The hive also applies idempotently on (source_node_id, source_task_id), so\n156:         // distinct keys across writes of the same task are safe. \"Deterministic\" is not an SC\n157:         // requirement — only per-write uniqueness + stable-per-row.\n158:         let op = NewOutboxOp {\n159:             op_type: \"task.upsert\".to_string(),\n160:             entity_type: \"task\".to_string(),\n161:             entity_id: task.id,\n162:             payload,\n163:             idempotency_key: format!(\"task:{}:{}\", task.id, Uuid::new_v4()),\n164:             fencing_token: None,\n165:         };\n166:         if let Err(e) = OutboxRepository::enqueue_op(pool, op).await {\n167:             tracing::warn!(error = %e, task_id = %task.id, \"failed to enqueue task.upsert op (legacy sync is the backstop)\");\n168:         }\n169:     }\n170: ```\n171: \n172: ## Allowed moves\n173: ONLY: rebind the `create`/`update` query results to `let task = …await?;`, append the\n174: `enqueue_task_upsert_op` call + `Ok(task)`, and add the one private `enqueue_task_upsert_op` helper.
