The op payload is the synced task shape; for the tracer, serialize the\n  returned `Task` row itself (`serde_json::to_value(&task)`) — the hive's `upsert_from_node` (106) reads\n  the fields it needs.\n  Each edit is TWO literal changes: bind the `query_as!` result with `let task =`, and replace the\n  trailing `.await` with `.await?; … Ok(task)`.\n- **Before (`create`, the `query_as!` opening @268):**\n```rust\n        sqlx::query_as!(\n            Task,\n```\n- **After:**\n```rust\n        let task = sqlx::query_as!(\n            Task,\n```\n- **Before (`create` tail, @290-292):**\n```rust\n        )\n        .fetch_one(pool)\n        .await\n    }\n```\n- **After:**\n```rust\n        )\n        .fetch_one(pool)\n        .await?;\n        Self::enqueue_task_upsert_op(pool, &task).await;\n        Ok(task)\n    }\n```\n- **Before (`update`, the `query_as!` opening @303):**\n```rust\n        sqlx::query_as!(\n            Task,\n```\n- **After:**\n```rust\n        let task = sqlx::query_as!(\n            Task,\n```\n  > CRITICAL: `sqlx::query_as!(\\n            Task,` appears SIX times in this file (@167,188,213,241,268,303).\n  > Rebind `let task =` ONLY at the `create` (@268) and `update` (@303) occurrences — the other four are\n  > SELECT methods using `.fetch_optional`/`.fetch_all` and MUST NOT be touched. Anchor by line, not by\n  > the (non-unique) text. The `.fetch_one(pool)` tail IS unique to create/update (only @290,@325), so\n  > the tail Before/After is unambiguous — but the `let task =` opener is not; pair them by proximity.\n- **Before (`update` tail, @325-327):**\n```rust\n        )\n        .fetch_one(pool)\n        .await\n    }\n```\n- **After:**\n```rust\n        )\n        .fetch_one(pool)\n        .await?;\n        Self::enqueue_task_upsert_op(pool, &task).await;\n        Ok(task)\n    }\n```\n  > Both `create` and `update` also end with the IDENTICAL `)\\n        .fetch_one(pool)\\n        .await\\n    }`\n  > tail — apply the rebind to BOTH (they are the only two such tails in this impl after the SELECTs,\n  > which use `.fetch_optional`/`.fetch_all`; verify before editing).\n- **Add a private helper** on `impl Task` (top of the impl block or just below `update`):\n```rust\n    /// Enqueue a `task.upsert` op into node_outbox alongside the local write (SC2 tracer).\n    /// Runs ALONGSIDE the legacy hive_sync path (additive; hive apply is idempotent). Best-effort:\n    /// a failed enqueue is logged, NOT propagated — the legacy path remains the backstop, and the\n    /// enqueue is a separate statement from the task write (not one txn), so a crash between them is\n    /// covered by the legacy sync. (Threading a shared txn through all Task::create callers is OUT of\n    /// scope for the tracer — see decisions-ledger.)\n    async fn enqueue_task_upsert_op(pool: &SqlitePool, task: &Task) {\n        use crate::models::node_outbox::{NewOutboxOp, OutboxRepository};\n        let payload = match serde_json::to_value(task) {\n            Ok(v) => v,\n            Err(e) => { tracing::warn!(error = %e, task_id = %task.id, \"skip outbox enqueue: serialize failed\"); return; }\n        };\n        // Per-write-unique idempotency key. DELIBERATELY NOT `task:{id}:{version}`: Task::update does\n        // NOT bump any version column (queries.rs UPDATE sets only title/description/status/parent_task_id),\n        // so a version-only key collides on every update and the UNIQUE(idempotency_key) constraint\n        // would silently drop the update op. A fresh Uuid suffix is assigned ONCE here and persisted\n        // with the row, so a re-transmit of the SAME outbox row reuses the SAME key and the hive dedups\n        // (node_op_log PK). The hive also applies idempotently on (source_node_id, source_task_id), so\n        // distinct keys across writes of the same task are safe. \"Deterministic\" is not an SC\n        // requirement — only per-write uniqueness + stable-per-row.\n        let op = NewOutboxOp {\n            op_type: \"task.upsert\".to_string(),\n            entity_type: \"task\".to_string(),\n            entity_id: task.id,\n            payload,\n            idempotency_key: format!(\"task:{}:{}\", task.id, Uuid::new_v4()),\n            fencing_token: None,\n        };\n        if let Err(e) = OutboxRepository::enqueue_op(pool, op).await {\n            tracing::warn!(error = %e, task_id = %task.id, \"failed to enqueue task.upsert op (legacy sync is the backstop)\");\n        }\n    }\n```\n\n## Allowed moves\nONLY: rebind the `create`/`update` query results to `let task = …await?;`, append the\n`enqueue_task_upsert_op` call + `Ok(task)`, and add the one private `enqueue_task_upsert_op` helper. Do\nNOT change `Task::create`/`Task::update` public signatures or return types, do NOT remove/alter the\nlegacy `hive_sync` path, do NOT touch any other `impl Task` method, do NOT edit `node_outbox.rs` or\n`NewOutboxOp` (104 owns those).\n\n## STOP triggers\n- The real `CreateTask` struct fields differ from the test literal → adjust the test struct literal to\n  the actual `super::CreateTask` shape (do NOT change `CreateTask`).\n- `serde_json` is a CONFIRMED direct dep of `crates/db` (`crates/db/Cargo.toml:11`), so\n  `serde_json::to_value`/`json!` resolve without a new dep. There is NO shared `common` module (the\n`remote/tests/` dir holds only `backfill_e2e.rs` + `pool_config.rs`) — inline the helpers.\n\nAdd to `session.rs`:\n```rust\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod op_batch_tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    fn database_url() -> Option<String> { std::env::var(\"DATABASE_URL\").ok() }\n    macro_rules! skip_without_db { () => {\n        if database_url().is_none() { eprintln!(\"Skipping: DATABASE_URL not set\"); return; }\n    }; }\n    async fn create_pool() -> sqlx::PgPool {\n        sqlx::PgPool::connect(&database_url().unwrap()).await.expect(\"connect\")\n    }\n    // … inline create_test_organization / create_test_node / seed a swarm_project + node_local_projects\n    //    link exactly as backfill_e2e.rs seeds them.\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn op_batch_applies_swarm_linked_task_idempotently_and_acks() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        // seed org, node, swarm_project, node_local_projects(node_id, local_project_id, swarm_project_id).\n        // op = OutboxOp { seq:1, op_type:\"task.upsert\", entity_type:\"task\", entity_id: local_task_id,\n        //   payload: serde_json::json!({\"id\": local_task_id, \"project_id\": local_project_id,\n        //   \"title\":\"t\", \"description\": null, \"status\":\"done\"}), idempotency_key:\"task:..:..\", fencing_token:None }\n        // Apply twice (build a no-op ack sink — see STOP note on ws_sender in test):\n        //   1st: node_op_log gets exactly one row; shared_tasks has the task; applied_through_seq == 1.\n        //   2nd: node_op_log still ONE row (ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING); no error; applied_through_seq == 1.\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn op_batch_PARKS_when_local_project_link_absent() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        // seed org+node but NO node_local_projects row → TRANSIENT (ProjectsSync race).\n        // op seq:1 for that missing project. Apply: applied_through_seq does NOT advance to 1\n        // (stays at high-water 0), and node_op_log has NO row for the key → the node re-sends it.\n    }\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn op_batch_SKIPS_AND_ADVANCES_when_project_present_but_not_swarm_linked() {\n        skip_without_db!();\n        let pool = create_pool().await;\n        // seed node_local_projects row WITHOUT swarm_project_id (or no swarm_project_nodes link) →\n        // PERMANENT (project intentionally not swarm-linked). Apply: applied_through_seq DOES advance\n        // to 1 (the op is acked/skipped, NOT parked) and node_op_log records it — so a non-swarm task\n        // at the outbox head does NOT wedge the cursor forever.\n    }\n}\n```\n> The third test is the wedge guard. Without the park-vs-skip split (below), a single non-swarm task at\n> the outbox head would park permanently and the op-log would never advance for that node.\n\n## Change\n- **File:** `crates/remote/src/nodes/ws/session.rs`\n- **Anchor:** the `NodeMessage::OpBatch { ops }` STUB arm added by 103 in `handle_node_message`\n  (@~580-585 after 103 lands), plus a NEW `handle_op_batch` fn placed beside `handle_task_sync` (@1547).\n- **Sibling read (rubric #9):** `handle_task_sync` (@1547-1727) is the apply+reply template AND the\n  authority on park-vs-skip. It resolves context in three steps that ALREADY distinguish transient from\n  permanent — copy that exactly:\n  1. `NodeLocalProjectRepository::find_by_node_and_project` returns `None` (@1577-1599) → **TRANSIENT**\n     (ProjectsSync race): `handle_task_sync` replies \"RETRY\". For the op-log → **PARK** (break, no advance).\n  2. row present but `local_project.swarm_project_id` is `None` (@1603-1626) → **PERMANENT** (not linked):\n     `handle_task_sync` replies \"link via UI\". For the op-log → **SKIP + ADVANCE** (treat like the\n     `op_type != \"task.upsert\"` guard — ack it; do NOT wedge the cursor).\n  3. `swarm_project_nodes`/`swarm_projects` org lookup returns `None` (@1629-1667) → **PERMANENT** (bad\n     link): also **SKIP + ADVANCE**.\n  Ack reuses the `HeartbeatAck` send shape (@604-612).\n- **Before (the 103 stub arm):**\n```rust\n        NodeMessage::OpBatch { ops } => {\n            // STUB — filled by task 106 (idempotent apply + durable OpAck). Logs so the exhaustive\n            // match compiles now; 106 replaces the body with handle_op_batch(...).\n            tracing::debug!(node_id = %node_id, op_count = ops.len(), \"received op_batch (apply TODO: task 106)\");\n            Ok(())\n        }\n```\n- **After:**\n```rust\n        NodeMessage::OpBatch { ops } => {\n            handle_op_batch(node_id, organization_id, node_name, ops, pool, ws_sender).await\n        }\n```\n- **Add `handle_op_batch`** (new fn beside `handle_task_sync`). EXACT contract:\n  - Signature mirrors `handle_task_sync` PLUS the `ops` vec:\n    `async fn handle_op_batch(node_id: Uuid, organization_id: Uuid, node_name: &str, ops: Vec<OutboxOp>,\n    pool: &PgPool, ws_sender: &mut SplitSink<WebSocket, Message>) -> Result<(), HandleError>`\n    (`OutboxOp` = `crate::nodes::ws::message::OutboxOp` from 103).\n  - `applied_through_seq` starts at the node's current high-water:\n    `SELECT COALESCE(MAX(seq),0) FROM node_op_log WHERE node_id = $1`.\n  - Iterate `ops` IN ORDER. For each op:\n    - **(a) Tracer scope guard:** `op.op_type != \"task.upsert\"` → SKIP + `applied_through_seq = op.seq`\n      (later increments add other op types). Continue.\n    - **(b) Resolve context (copy `handle_task_sync` @1569-1667):**\n      - `find_by_node_and_project(pool, node_id, payload.project_id)` is `None` → **PARK**: `break` (do\n        NOT advance, do NOT insert node_op_log). TRANSIENT — re-sent after ProjectsSync. Log debug.\n      - row present but `swarm_project_id` is `None`, OR the swarm-link/org query is `None` → **SKIP +\n        ADVANCE**: `applied_through_seq = op.seq`; record it in node_op_log (so the high-water reflects\n        it); do NOT call `upsert_from_node`. PERMANENT (not swarm-linked) — must NOT wedge the cursor.\n        Continue.\n    - **(c) Idempotent apply (context present + swarm-linked):**\n      `INSERT INTO node_op_log (node_id, idempotency_key, seq, op_type, entity_id) VALUES (..)\n       ON CONFLICT (node_id, idempotency_key) DO NOTHING` → `rows_affected`.\n      - `rows_affected == 1` (first time): `SharedTaskRepository::upsert_from_node(UpsertTaskFromNodeData\n        { swarm_project_id, project_id: swarm_project_id, organization_id: org_id, origin_node_id:\n        node_id, local_task_id: payload.id, title, description, status, version: 1, owner_node_id:\n        Some(node_id), owner_name: Some(node_name.to_string()), assignee_user_id: None })` (construction\n        identical to `handle_task_sync` @1675).\n      - `rows_affected == 0` (already applied): skip the upsert (idempotent).\n      - Either branch: `applied_through_seq = op.seq`.\n  - After the loop: `send_message(ws_sender, &HiveMessage::OpAck { applied_through_seq }).await\n    .map_err(|_| HandleError::Send)?;` (always send). Return `Ok(())`.\n  > For the SKIP+ADVANCE permanent cases (b), recording the op in node_op_log keeps the cursor and the\n  > dedup table consistent (a re-sent permanent-skip op stays deduped). The PARK case (transient) is the\n  > ONLY one that does not advance.\n\n## Allowed moves\nONLY: replace the 103 `OpBatch` stub body with the `handle_op_batch(...)` call, add the `handle_op_batch`\nfn (apply + ack with the park-vs-skip split above), and add the `#[cfg(test)] mod op_batch_tests`. Reuse\n`send_message`, `SharedTaskRepository`, `NodeLocalProjectRepository`, `UpsertTaskFromNodeData`, and the\nswarm-link queries — do NOT re-implement them. Do NOT touch the WS enum definitions (103 owns them), the\nnode side, or any migration. Does NOT mark them acked — the cursor advances only on the hive's durable OpAck\n        // (task 108). Runs ALONGSIDE the legacy sync above (additive; hive apply is idempotent).\n        if let Err(e) = self.sync_outbox().await {\n            warn!(error = ?e, \"Failed to drain node_outbox op-log\");\n        }\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Drain unacked node_outbox ops and push them to the hive as one ordered `OpBatch`.\n    /// Best-effort: an empty outbox sends nothing. Does NOT advance the ack cursor (108 owns that).\n    async fn sync_outbox(&self) -> Result<(), HiveSyncError> {\n        use db::models::node_outbox::OutboxRepository;\n        let rows = OutboxRepository::peek_unacked(&self.pool, self.config.max_tasks_per_batch).await?;\n        if rows.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n        let ops: Vec<OutboxOp> = rows\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|r| OutboxOp {\n                seq: r.seq,\n                op_type: r.op_type,\n                entity_type: r.entity_type,\n                entity_id: r.entity_id,\n                payload: r.payload,\n                idempotency_key: r.idempotency_key,\n                fencing_token: r.fencing_token,\n            })\n            .collect();\n        self.command_tx\n            .send(NodeMessage::OpBatch { ops })\n            .await\n            .map_err(|e| HiveSyncError::Send(e.to_string()))?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n```\n\n## Allowed moves\nONLY: add `OutboxOp` to the import, call `self.sync_outbox()` at the end of `sync_once`, and add the\nprivate `sync_outbox` helper that peeks unacked rows and sends ONE `OpBatch`. Do NOT mark ops acked here\n(108 owns the cursor advance on `OpAck`), do NOT remove/alter the existing legacy `sync_*` calls, do NOT\nchange `sync_once`'s signature.\n\n## STOP triggers\n- `db::models::node_outbox::OutboxRepository`/the db-row `OutboxOp` fields differ from 104 → 104 must be\n  `passed`; align field names. HiveClientError::Serde(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        match hive_msg {\n            HiveMessage::TaskAssign(assign) => {\n                tracing::info!(\n                    assignment_id = self.event_tx.send(HiveEvent::TaskAssigned(assign)).await;\n            }\n            HiveMessage::TaskCancel(cancel) => {\n                tracing::info!(\n                    assignment_id = %cancel.assignment_id,\n                    \"received task cancellation\"\n                );\n                let _ = self.event_tx.send(HiveEvent::TaskCancelled(cancel)).await;\n            }\n ?response.error,\n                        \"task sync failed\"\n                    );\n                }\n                let _ = self\n                    .event_tx\n futures::stream::SplitSink<WebSocket, Message>,\n    last_heartbeat: &mut chrono::DateTime<Utc>,\n    tracker: &BackfillRequestTracker,\n) -> Result<(), HandleError> {\n    match msg {\n        NodeMessage::Heartbeat(heartbeat) => {\n            handle_heartbeat(\n                node_id,\n                heartbeat,\n                pool,\n                connections,\n                ws_sender,\n                last_heartbeat,\n            )\n            .await\n        }\n        NodeMessage::TaskStatus(status) => {\n            handle_task_status(node_id, organization_id, status, pool).await\n        }\n        NodeMessage::TaskOutput(output) => handle_task_output(node_id, output, pool).await,\n        NodeMessage::TaskProgress(progress) => handle_task_progress(node_id, progress, pool).await,\n        NodeMessage::LinkProject(link) => {\n            handle_link_project(node_id, organization_id, link, pool, connections).await\n        }\n        NodeMessage::UnlinkProject(unlink) => {\n            handle_unlink_project(node_id, organization_id, unlink, pool, connections).await\n        }\n        NodeMessage::Deregister(deregister) => {\n            handle_deregister(node_id, organization_id, deregister, pool, connections).await\n        }\n        NodeMessage::AttemptSync(attempt) => handle_attempt_sync(node_id, attempt, pool).await,\n        NodeMessage::ExecutionSync(execution) => {\n            handle_execution_sync(node_id, execution, pool).await\n        }\n        NodeMessage::LogsBatch(logs) => handle_logs_batch(node_id, logs, pool).await,\n        NodeMessage::LabelSync(_label) => {\n            // Labels are no longer synced from nodes to hive.\n            // Labels are managed centrally on the hive and synced DOWN to nodes.\n            // Ignore incoming label sync messages from nodes.\n            tracing::debug!(\n                node_id = %node_id,\n                \"ignoring deprecated label sync from node - labels are now hive-managed\"\n            );\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        NodeMessage::TaskSync(task) => {\n            handle_task_sync(node_id, organization_id, node_name, task, pool, ws_sender).await\n        }\n        NodeMessage::ProjectsSync(projects) => handle_projects_sync(node_id, projects, pool).await,\n        NodeMessage::Ack { message_id } => {\n            tracing::trace!(node_id = %node_id, message_id = %message_id, \"received ack\");\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        NodeMessage::Error { message_id, error } => {\n            tracing::warn!(\n                node_id = %node_id,\n                message_id = ?message_id,\n                error = %error,\n                \"received error from node\"\n            );\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        NodeMessage::Auth(_) => {\n            // Auth should only happen once at connection start\n            tracing::warn!(node_id = %node_id, \"received unexpected auth message\");\n            Ok(())\n        }\n        NodeMessage::BackfillResponse(response) => {\n            handle_backfill_response(node_id, response, pool, tracker).await\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Handle a heartbeat message.\nasync fn handle_heartbeat(\n    node_id: Uuid,\n    heartbeat: &HeartbeatMessage,\n    pool: &PgPool,\n    connections: &ConnectionManager,\n    ws_sender: &mut futures::stream::SplitSink<WebSocket, Message>,\n    last_heartbeat: &mut chrono::DateTime<Utc>,\n) -> Result<(), HandleError> fully linked → proceed with sync\nasync fn handle_task_sync(\n    node_id: Uuid,\n    organization_id: Uuid,\n    node_name: &str,\n    task_sync: &TaskSyncMessage,\n    pool: &PgPool,\n    ws_sender: &mut futures::stream::SplitSink<WebSocket, Message>,\n) -> Result<(), HandleError> {\n    use crate::db::node_local_projects::NodeLocalProjectRepository;\n    use crate::db::tasks::{SharedTaskRepository, TaskStatus, UpsertTaskFromNodeData};\n\n    let status = match task_sync.status.as_str() {\n        \"todo\" => TaskStatus::Todo,\n        \"in_progress\" | \"in-progress\" => TaskStatus::InProgress,\n        \"in_review\" | \"in-review\" => TaskStatus::InReview,\n        \"done\" => TaskStatus::Done,\n        \"cancelled\" => TaskStatus::Cancelled,\n        _ => TaskStatus::Todo,\n    };\n\n    // First check if the node_local_projects record exists\n    // This distinguishes between \"ProjectsSync hasn't arrived\" and \"project not linked\"\n    let local_project = NodeLocalProjectRepository::find_by_node_and_project(\n        pool,\n        node_id,\n        task_sync.local_project_id,\n    )\n    .await\n    .map_err(|e| HandleError::Database(e.to_string()))?;\n\n    let local_project = match local_project {\n        Some(p) => p,\n        None => {\n            // Race condition: ProjectsSync hasn't arrived yet\n            // Tell the node to retry after its ProjectsSync completes\n            tracing::debug!(\n                node_id = %node_id,\n                local_project_id = %task_sync.local_project_id,\n                local_task_id = %task_sync.local_task_id,\n                \"task sync: project not found in node_local_projects (ProjectsSync race, retry)\"\n            );\n            let r = local_task_id = %task_sync.local_task_id,\n                \"task sync: project not linked to swarm (link via UI first)\"\n            );\n            let r = TaskSyncResponseMessage {\n - link it via the swarm settings UI first\"\n                        .to_string(),\n                ),\n            };\n            let _ = send_message(ws_sender, &HiveMessage::TaskSyncResponse(r)).await;\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n    };\n\n    // Verify the swarm project belongs to this organization and node has a link\n    let swarm_link: Option<SwarmProjectLink> = sqlx::query_as(\n        r#\"\n        SELECT\n            sp.organization_id\n        FROM swarm_project_nodes spn\n        JOIN swarm_projects sp ON spn.swarm_project_id = sp.id\n        WHERE spn.node_id = $1\n          AND spn.local_project_id = $2\n          AND spn.swarm_project_id = $3\n          AND sp.organization_id = $4\n        \"#,\n    )\n    .bind(node_id)\n    .bind(task_sync.local_project_id)\n    .bind(swarm_project_id)\n    .bind(organization_id)\n    .fetch_optional(pool)\n    .await\n    .map_err(|e| HandleError::Database(e.to_string()))?;\n\n    let org_id = match swarm_link {\n        Some(link) => link.organization_id,\n        None => {\n            tracing::warn!(\n                node_id = or org mismatch\"\n            );\n            let r = TaskSyncResponseMessage {\n                local_task_id: task_sync.local_task_id,\n                shared_task_id: Uuid::nil(),\n .clone()\n                .or_else(|| Some(node_name.to_string())),\n            assignee_user_id: task_sync.assignee_user_id,\n        })\n        .await\n    {\n        Ok((task, was_created)) => db::models::task::Task;\nuse db::models::task_attempt::TaskAttempt;\nuse sqlx::SqlitePool;\nuse tokio::sync::mpsc;\nuse tokio::time::{self, MissedTickBehavior};\nuse tracing::{debug, error, info, warn};\nuse uuid::Uuid;\n\nuse super::hive_client::{\n    AttemptSyncMessage, ExecutionSyncMessage, LocalProjectSyncInfo, LogsBatchMessage, NodeMessage,\n    ProjectsSyncMessage, SyncLogEntry, TaskOutputType, TaskSyncMessage,\n};\n\n/// Configuration for the Hive sync service.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct HiveSyncConfig {\n    /// How often to check for unsynced entities\n    pub sync_interval: Duration,\n    /// Maximum number of tasks to sync in one batch\n    pub max_tasks_per_batch: i64,\n    /// Maximum number of attempts to sync in one batch\n    pub max_attempts_per_batch: i64,\n    /// Maximum number of executions to sync in one batch\n    pub max_executions_per_batch: i64,\n    /// Maximum number of log entries to sync in one batch\n    pub max_logs_per_batch: i64,\n}\n\nimpl Default for HiveSyncConfig {\n    /// Creates a HiveSyncConfig populated with sensible defaults for the Hive sync service.\n    ///\n    /// Defaults:\n    /// - `sync_interval`: 30 seconds\n    /// - `max_tasks_per_batch`: 50\n    /// - `max_attempts_per_batch`: 50\n    /// - `max_executions_per_batch`: 100\n    /// - `max_logs_per_batch`: 500\n    ///\n    /// # Examples\n    ///\n    /// ```\n    /// let cfg = HiveSyncConfig::default();\n    /// assert_eq!(cfg.sync_interval, std::time::Duration::from_secs(30));\n    /// assert_eq!(cfg.max_tasks_per_batch, 50);\n    /// assert_eq!(cfg.max_attempts_per_batch, 50);\n    /// assert_eq!(cfg.max_executions_per_batch, 100);\n    /// assert_eq!(cfg.max_logs_per_batch, 500);\n    /// ```\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            // 30 seconds is appropriate for project/task sync\n            // Active execution (logs/attempts) happens more frequently via direct messages\n            sync_interval: Duration::from_secs(30),\n            max_tasks_per_batch: 50,\n            max_attempts_per_batch: 50,\n            max_executions_per_batch: 100,\n            max_logs_per_batch: 500,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Errors from the Hive sync service.\n#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]\npub enum HiveSyncError {\n    #[error(\"database error: {0}\")]\n    Database(#[from] sqlx::Error),\n    #[error(\"send error: {0}\")]\n    Send(String),\n    #[error(\"task not found for attempt: {0}\")]\n    TaskNotFound(Uuid),\n    #[error(\"task not linked to Hive: {0}\")]\n    TaskNotLinked(Uuid),\n}\n\n/// Service for syncing local entities to the Hive.\npub struct HiveSyncService {\n    pool: SqlitePool,\n    command_tx: mpsc::Sender<NodeMessage>,\n    config: HiveSyncConfig,\n}\n\nimpl HiveSyncService {\n    /// Create a new Hive sync service.\n    pub fn new(\n        pool: SqlitePool,\n        command_tx: mpsc::Sender<NodeMessage>,\n        config: HiveSyncConfig,\n    ) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            pool,\n            command_tx,\n            config,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Run the sync service in a loop.\n    ///\n    /// This spawns a background task that periodically syncs unsynced entities.\n    /// The task runs until the channel is closed.\n    pub fn spawn(self) -> tokio::task::JoinHandle<()> {\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            let mut interval = time::interval(self.config.sync_interval);\n            interval.set_missed_tick_behavior(MissedTickBehavior::Skip);\n\n            loop {\n                interval.tick().await;\n\n                if let Err(e) = self.sync_once().await {\n                    warn!(error = ?e, \"Hive sync cycle failed\");\n                }\n            }\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Perform one sync cycle.\n    ///\n    /// This syncs local projects first (so hive knows available projects), then\n    /// tasks (to get shared_task_id), then attempts, executions, and logs in order.\n    ///\n    /// Note: Labels are NOT synced from nodes to hive. Labels are managed centrally\n    /// on the hive and synced DOWN to nodes via the auth response and broadcast messages.\n    pub async fn sync_once(&self) -> Result<(), HiveSyncError> {\n        // Sync local projects first (so hive knows what's available on this node)\n        if let Err(e) = self.sync_local_projects().await {\n            // Log but don't fail the entire sync - other syncs can continue\n            warn!(error = ?e, \"Failed to sync local projects\");\n        }\n\n        // Sync tasks first (to ensure shared_task_id exists for attempts)\n        let tasks_synced = self.sync_tasks().await?;\n        if tasks_synced > 0 {\n            debug!(count = tasks_synced, \"Synced tasks to Hive\");\n        }\n\n        // Sync attempts next (parent entities for executions)\n        let attempts_synced = self.sync_attempts().await?;\n        if attempts_synced > 0 {\n            debug!(count = attempts_synced, \"Synced task attempts to Hive\");\n        }\n\n        // Sync executions next\n        let executions_synced = self.sync_executions().await?;\n        if executions_synced > 0 {\n            debug!(\n                count = executions_synced,\n                \"Synced execution processes to Hive\"\n            );\n        }\n\n        // Sync logs\n        let logs_synced = self.sync_logs().await?;\n        if logs_synced > 0 {\n            debug!(count = logs_synced, \"Synced log entries to Hive\");\n        }\n\n        // Labels are NOT synced from nodes to hive - they flow hive->nodes only\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Synchronizes local tasks that require a Hive-side shared_task_id.\n    ///\n    /// This finds tasks that:\n    /// 1. Don't have a shared_task_id (new tasks)\n    /// 2. Have shared_task_id but need resync (remote_last_synced_at IS NULL)\n    /// 3. Belong to local projects (not remote) with a remote_project_id (linked to swarm)\n    ///\n    /// This includes:\n    /// - Tasks created before the project was linked to swarm\n    /// - Tasks that failed initial sync\n    /// - Tasks without any attempts yet\n    /// - Tasks marked for force resync via mark_for_resync_by_project\n    ///\n    /// # Returns\n    ///\n    /// The number of tasks for which a `TaskSync` message was sent.\n    ///\n    /// # Examples\n    ///\n    /// ```no_run\n    /// // `service` is an instance of `HiveSyncService`.\n    /// # async fn example(service: &crate::hive::HiveSyncService) {\n    /// let synced = service.sync_tasks().await.unwrap();\n    /// println!(\"sent {} task sync messages\", synced);\n    /// # }\n    /// ```\n    async fn sync_tasks(&self) -> Result<usize, HiveSyncError> {\n        // Find ALL tasks in swarm-linked projects that are missing shared_task_id\n        // This captures tasks created before project was linked, failed syncs, etc.\n        let mut tasks =\n            Task::find_missing_shared_task_id(&self.pool, self.config.max_tasks_per_batch).await?;\n\n        // Also find tasks that have shared_task_id but need resync (force resync scenario)\n        let resync_tasks =\n            Task::find_needing_resync(&self.pool, self.config.max_tasks_per_batch).await?;\n        tasks.extend(resync_tasks);\n\n        if tasks.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(0);\n        }","lineStart":30,"lineEnd":229,"totalLines":656,"truncated":true}},"title":"crates/services/src/services/hive_sync.rs","time":{"start":1782821271939,"end":1782821271943}},"id":"prt_f186db9800014jzlLCutUOGUet","sessionID":"ses_0e793c9a1ffeiLk31zpbRPWbnP","messageID":"msg_f186d942f002k5XOFpgzmhQdm8"}}
